# Maestro — Web Application over Tailscale (Trillium's Fork)

> Project ISA. Source of truth for this fork's deviation from upstream. Lives in repo, reviewed in PRs, outlives any single task run.
>
> **Upstream stays Electron. This fork repoints the primary surface to a Tailscale-hosted web app.**

## Problem

Upstream Maestro ships as an Electron 28 desktop app. The principal (Trillium) works across multiple machines (laptop, mini2, mini3, phone) connected over Tailscale and wants ONE running Maestro instance reachable from any of them via a browser. Electron pins the runtime to a single host: the app is wherever the principal last clicked the dock icon, requires per-machine installs, per-machine state, per-machine updates, and cannot be reached from phone or non-Mac devices.

The friction this causes: context-loss when moving between machines, multiple stale instances diverging on state, mobile-from-bed access blocked, mini2/mini3 (the always-on hosts) not utilized. Upstream already has a substantial web target (`src/web/`, `src/main/web-server/` running Fastify on 45678, `vite.config.web.mts`), but Electron is still the launcher and several subsystems (`node-pty` terminals, `better-sqlite3` DB, `electron-store` settings, `electron-updater`) assume the Electron process model.

## Vision

One Maestro instance runs on mini2 (the always-on Mac in Trillium's tailnet). Trillium opens `http://mini2.<tailnet>.ts.net:45678` from his laptop's browser, his iPhone, or any borrowed machine that's joined to the tailnet, and gets the same Maestro UI — same active sessions, same terminal scrollback, same database, same settings, same in-flight conversations. No installs. No "which copy of Maestro has my work in it." Tailscale handles network reachability AND identity (if you're on the tailnet, you're Trillium). Closing the laptop lid does not lose any work. Mobile access is good enough to read/respond from a phone.

Euphoric surprise on convergence: Trillium opens the app on his phone in bed, sees a terminal he started from his laptop at the office still streaming output, taps it, dictates a command, and watches it execute — all without thinking about where "the app" is.

## Out of Scope

- **Multi-tenant SaaS.** Not building user accounts, billing, workspace isolation, or per-tenant data segregation. Single user (Trillium) is the design assumption forever.
- **Public-internet exposure.** No public TLS, no Cloudflare tunnel, no OAuth. Tailscale identity = auth. If reverse-proxying is ever needed it is a separate sub-project.
- **Electron parity for upstream.** This fork does NOT promise to keep Electron builds passing CI. Upstream owns the desktop product; this fork is a web-first divergence.
- **Native mobile apps.** No iOS/Android wrappers. Mobile = mobile-responsive web served from the same Fastify origin (`src/web/mobile/` already exists per repo scan).
- **Maintaining `dmg`/`AppImage`/`nsis` packaging targets.** These can rot in this fork; PRs upstream-only.
- **Auto-update via electron-updater.** Replaced by `git pull && bun run build:web && systemd/launchd restart` on the host.

## Principles

1. **Tailscale is the perimeter.** Anything reachable on the tailnet is reachable by Trillium and nobody else; we trust that for auth and transport. No re-implementing identity inside the app.
2. **State lives once, on the host.** SQLite file, electron-store equivalents, session files — all on mini2's disk. Every browser session is a thin client into that state. Conflict resolution for "two browsers editing the same thing" is last-writer-wins via WebSocket events.
3. **Terminal sessions are server-owned.** `node-pty` ptys live in the server process, persist across browser disconnects, stream over WebSocket to xterm.js (or whatever upstream's renderer uses). Closing a tab does NOT kill the pty.
4. **Mobile responsiveness is first-class, not a bolt-on.** `src/web/mobile/` already exists; keep it healthy.
5. **Don't fork code, fork posture.** Stay close enough to upstream that periodic `git pull` from RunMaestro is mechanical. Divergence lives in adapters, launcher scripts, build targets — not in business logic.
6. **Server-side native modules stay.** `better-sqlite3` and `node-pty` keep running in the Node process; we don't replace them, we just stop wrapping the process in Electron.

## Constraints

- **`src/web/` is read-only on this fork.** Never edit, refactor, rename, lint-fix, or auto-format any file under `src/web/`. Treated as a verbatim mirror of upstream `RunMaestro/Maestro` so `git pull upstream main` is mechanical. All divergent web-UI work — including bugfixes to the mobile-companion surface — happens in `src/webFull/` (created from `src/web/` on 2026-06-07, commit `ee6274e1f`). This constraint is non-negotiable per Trillium's standing rule (2026-06-07). Anti-criterion ISC-43 enforces.
- **Node ≥22** (upstream `engines`). Host is macOS (mini2 / mini3), arm64.
- **Tailscale must be the only network path in the v1 deploy.** No `0.0.0.0` binding on a public IP.
- **Stay rebase-friendly with upstream `RunMaestro/Maestro main`.** Avoid invasive edits to files upstream touches frequently; prefer adapter/launcher files.
- **Single user, but possibly multiple concurrent browser tabs/devices.** WebSocket session model must tolerate N clients on one server.
- **Existing IPC contract is load-bearing.** `src/main/web-server/web-server-factory.ts` already bridges HTTP/WS → IPC `ipcMain.once(responseChannel, ...)`. Repointing requires either keeping the IPC stub or rewriting the bridge to direct in-process calls.
- **node-pty + better-sqlite3 native rebuilds** must work against the actual Node version running the standalone server. Cannot mix Electron's ABI with vanilla Node's ABI on the same `node_modules/`.
- **`@sentry/electron` does not run outside Electron.** Replace with `@sentry/node` or strip in the web build.
- **`electron-store` does not run outside Electron.** Replace with a `~/.config/maestro/settings.json` shim or migrate to the existing SQLite.

## Goal

Deliver a `bun run start:web` (or equivalent) launch path that runs Maestro's Fastify+WebSocket server as a vanilla Node process on mini2, serves the prebuilt `dist/web/` SPA, exposes `/api` + `/ws` on a Tailscale-reachable port (45678 or chosen), survives browser disconnects, persists state to disk, and produces the same UX Trillium gets from `bun run dev` today — accessed from any browser on his tailnet. Electron remains buildable upstream-side for anyone who wants it, but is not on the critical path for this fork.

## Criteria

> **DRAFT.** Background research agent's web-port codebase conversion assessment ([brain-tlak](~/data/knowledge/entries/knowledge/maestro-web-port-codebase-conversion-assessment.md)) contains the full IPC inventory, native-module map, and tiered effort estimate. The granular ISCs (target ≥128 at E4) will be appended as those findings get distilled into criteria here. Initial scaffold below covers the load-bearing structural criteria.

### Tier 1 — local web parity (laptop → laptop, same machine)

- [ ] ISC-1: `npm install` completes on host without electron-rebuild failures for `node-pty` and `better-sqlite3` against vanilla Node 22+.
- [ ] ISC-2: `npm run build:web` produces `dist/web/` containing `index.html` + hashed JS/CSS assets and exits 0.
- [ ] ISC-3: A `start:web` script (to be added) launches a vanilla `node`/`bun` process (NOT `electron .`) that boots the Fastify server on a configurable port.
- [ ] ISC-4: With server running, `curl -i http://localhost:<port>/` returns 200 and the HTML body contains `<div id="root">` (or whatever upstream uses as the React root).
- [ ] ISC-5: With server running, `curl -i http://localhost:<port>/api/health` (or upstream equivalent) returns 200 with a JSON body — Interceptor screenshot of `/` shows the actual Maestro UI mounting in a real browser, not just bare HTML.
- [ ] ISC-6: WebSocket upgrade succeeds at `ws://localhost:<port>/ws` and a smoke handshake completes within 2s.
- [ ] ISC-7: `src/main/web-server/web-server-factory.ts` IPC bridge is either (a) kept working with an in-process stub OR (b) replaced with direct function calls — code path documented in Decisions.

### Tier 2 — Tailscale-hosted, multi-device

- [ ] ISC-8: Process runs as a launchd-managed service on mini2; survives reboot.
- [ ] ISC-9: Service binds to mini2's Tailscale interface (or `0.0.0.0` filtered by `tailscale serve` / firewall to tailnet-only). Anti: ISC-8 must NOT result in a public-internet listener.
- [ ] ISC-10: From laptop on tailnet, `https://mini2.<tailnet>.ts.net:<port>/` loads the UI in Chrome (Interceptor screenshot proof).
- [ ] ISC-11: From iPhone Safari on tailnet, the same URL loads `src/web/mobile/` variant and is usable (manual smoke test — checklist in Verification).
- [ ] ISC-12: Two browsers (laptop Chrome + phone Safari) connected simultaneously can both observe the SAME open terminal session; an action in one is reflected in the other within 1s via WebSocket.
- [ ] ISC-13: A running `node-pty` terminal survives a browser disconnect; reopening the URL re-attaches to the same pty with intact scrollback.
- [ ] ISC-14: Settings written from browser A are visible to browser B without an explicit reload (or after one reload — Decision called out).
- [ ] ISC-15: `better-sqlite3` DB file on mini2 is the single source of truth; no `~/Library/Application Support/Maestro` Electron-side artifacts are created during web-mode runtime.

### Anti-criteria & guard-rails

- [ ] ISC-16: Anti: web-mode server MUST NOT spawn an Electron `BrowserWindow` or require `electron` binary on the host PATH.
- [ ] ISC-17: Anti: no `0.0.0.0:<port>` binding on a host without Tailscale filtering — verified with `lsof -i :<port>` + `tailscale serve status`.
- [ ] ISC-18: Anti: no telemetry/auto-update beacons fire from the web-mode process to non-tailnet endpoints (network capture during a 60s idle).
- [ ] ISC-19: Anti: `@sentry/electron` MUST NOT be a runtime dep of `start:web` (verified by `lsof` / process tree).
- [ ] ISC-20: Anti: upstream `npm run dev` (Electron path) MUST still work — fork divergence MUST NOT brick the desktop dev loop for anyone rebasing.
- [ ] ISC-21: Antecedent: Tailscale daemon running on mini2 AND laptop AND phone before any Tier 2 ISC can be verified.
- [ ] ISC-45: **Falsification probe (post-L0c).** Antecedent: Layer 0c has landed and the headless server can spawn pty sessions from the browser. Probe: spawn a pty session from phone Safari against the mini2 server; send a command into it; observe output; `kill -9` the server process on mini2; restart the server (via launchd or `./infra/deploy.sh`); reload the phone tab; the SAME pty re-attaches with intact scrollback (the command and its output are still on-screen). If the pty does NOT survive — fresh terminal, no scrollback — the entire decouple-from-Electron investment delivered nothing the user can feel, and the project's value claim collapses regardless of which lower-numbered ISCs are green. Pairs with ISC-13 (the unit-level pty-persistence-across-disconnect criterion); ISC-45 is the integration-level "did the whole thing matter" check.

### Build & operational

- [ ] ISC-22: `bun run build:web` is reproducible — same git SHA produces identical `dist/web/` (modulo timestamps).
- [ ] ISC-23: `bun run lint` (or upstream's TS typecheck) stays green on this fork's added files.
- [ ] ISC-24: `bun run test` (or upstream's vitest) stays green on the web-server tests in `src/__tests__/main/web-server/`.
- [ ] ISC-25: A `README.fork.md` (or equivalent) at the repo root documents: how to install, how to launch in web mode, how to reach over Tailscale, how to rebase from upstream.
- [ ] ISC-26: `launchd` plist is checked into `infra/` (or similar) on this fork.
- [ ] ISC-27: A documented procedure for `git pull` from upstream + rebuild + restart exists.

### Agent-informed ISCs (replacing prior [PENDING] slots)

- [ ] ISC-28: A `src/server/index.ts` (or equivalent) headless bootstrap initializes `stores`, `ProcessManager`, `AgentDetector`, `HistoryManager`, `WebServer` WITHOUT importing `electron` or instantiating `BrowserWindow`. (Mirrors the `src/cli/` Node-only pattern that already exists.)
- [ ] ISC-29: `app.getPath('userData')` callsites (estimated ~10-20) are replaced with `process.env.MAESTRO_DATA_DIR ?? path.join(os.homedir(), '.config/maestro')`.
- [ ] ISC-30: All 42 `mainWindow.webContents.send(...)` callsites either route through `WebServer.broadcastService` or are deleted; web clients receive the same updates over WebSocket.
- [ ] ISC-31: `CallbackRegistry` is wired by the server itself in headless mode (replacing the renderer-round-trip that currently provides session callbacks).
- [ ] ISC-32: Desktop-only IPC handlers (`dialog:*`, `shell:*`, `devtools:*`, `power:*`, `tunnel:*`, `updates:*`, `clipboard:*`, `fonts:*`) are deleted or replaced with web-API equivalents in `src/server/` build, listed individually in Decisions.
- [ ] ISC-33: `@sentry/electron` is split: `@sentry/node` in `src/server/`, `@sentry/browser` in `src/web/`. Server process does not pull `@sentry/electron` at runtime.
- [ ] ISC-34: `electron-updater` is excluded from the server build (`src/main/auto-updater.ts` not imported by `src/server/index.ts`).
- [ ] ISC-35: `electron-devtools-installer` excluded from server build (it's already dev-only).
- [ ] ISC-36: `electron-store` is replaced with a file-based JSON store rooted at `MAESTRO_DATA_DIR`. The on-disk schema is preserved so a desktop-app data dir can be copied into web mode with no migration.
- [ ] ISC-37: Existing single-token-in-URL auth at `WebServer.ts:111-128` is retained as-is for Tier 1/2 over Tailscale — Anti: Tier 3 (multi-tenant) is excluded so no real-auth work this fork.
- [ ] ISC-38: chokidar watchers continue to operate, watching server-side workspace paths rather than client-chosen paths. Watch root configurable via `MAESTRO_WORKSPACE`.
- [ ] ISC-39: Service worker + PWA install banner at `/` are functional from a Tailscale URL (Interceptor probe on iPhone Safari, "Add to Home Screen" works).
- [ ] ISC-40: Rebase smoke — cleanly `git pull upstream main` and rebuild without conflict in non-`src/server/` files. (Bias edits to NEW files; minimize touches to upstream's `src/main/` and `src/main/web-server/`.)

### Scope decision required from principal (NEW after agent report)

- [ ] ISC-41: **Principal-decision-gated.** Either accept "browser UI is the mobile-companion surface (~mobile/App.tsx, no session-create, no agent-config, no file-browse, no git-diff, no Auto Run UI)" OR scope a Tier-1.5 to grow `src/web/` to cover desktop-class features. ANTI: must not silently regress desktop functionality without explicit acknowledgment.
- [ ] ISC-42: xterm.js + raw-byte WS multiplex SCOPED IN as Layer 6. Server-side multiplex shipped in L6.1 (sha `1e4b90e75`); client-side xterm renderer in L6.2 (in flight); scrollback disk persistence in L6.3. Status: server-half closed; client + persistence pending.
- [ ] ISC-43: **Anti: no commit on this fork modifies any file under `src/web/`.** Verified by `git log origin/main..HEAD -- src/web/` returning empty for any range under consideration. Auto-formatter runs, lint-fix sweeps, typo fixes — all forbidden. If a fix is needed, it happens in `src/webFull/`.

## Test Strategy

### Layer-0 / infrastructure ISCs

| ISC range | Probe type                         | Tool                                                                          | Threshold                                |
| --------- | ---------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| 1-3       | command exit code + file existence | `Bash`, `Read`                                                                | exit 0, file present                     |
| 4-6       | HTTP/WS probe                      | `curl -i`, WS smoke client                                                    | 2xx status, < 2s handshake               |
| 5, 10, 11 | live browser render                | `Skill("Interceptor")` screenshot at the URL                                  | UI visibly mounts, no console errors     |
| 7, 28-40  | code-level                         | `Read`, `Grep`, code review                                                   | bridge code path matches Decisions entry |
| 8         | launchd                            | `launchctl list \| grep maestro`, reboot smoke                                | service present, restarts on reboot      |
| 9, 17     | network surface                    | `lsof -i :<port>`, `tailscale serve status`, external `curl` from non-tailnet | bind matches policy                      |
| 12-14     | multi-client behavior              | two Interceptor sessions side-by-side                                         | state propagates < 1s                    |
| 13        | pty persistence                    | WS reconnect smoke after `kill -9` browser tab                                | scrollback intact                        |
| 16, 19    | process tree                       | `ps`, `lsof` against running server                                           | electron binary absent                   |
| 18        | egress                             | `tcpdump`/`Little Snitch` for 60s idle                                        | zero non-tailnet packets                 |
| 20        | upstream compat                    | `git checkout upstream/main && npm run dev` in worktree                       | Electron dev still launches              |
| 22        | reproducibility                    | hash dist/web twice from same SHA                                             | matches                                  |
| 23-24     | upstream tooling                   | `bun run lint`, `bun run test`                                                | exit 0                                   |
| 25-27     | docs presence                      | `Read`                                                                        | files exist with content                 |

### Per-feature function-parity ISCs (added when each port lands)

Every feature ported into `src/webFull/` gets a parity catalog at `src/webFull/<feature>/parity.test.ts` per the function-parity verification methodology ([brain-aq5m](~/data/knowledge/entries/knowledge/maestro-web-port-function-parity-verification-methodology.md)). The catalog is recorded against Electron at `localhost:9222` (the reference oracle), replayed against webFull at `localhost:5176`, and must pass on both. The allowed assertion types are `hasElement`, `hasText`, `wsFrameMatches`, `dbHasRow`, `fsHas`, `processHas`, `notificationFired`, `broadcast` — see [brain-aq5m](~/data/knowledge/entries/knowledge/maestro-web-port-function-parity-verification-methodology.md) for the full vocabulary and the standing "catalog is the spec, not the renderer source" rule. Per-feature ISCs will land in this ISA at the time each port commits, formatted as: `ISC-44.x: <feature-name> parity catalog passes against both Electron and webFull, ≥N stories, including ≥1 negative-path story per happy-path story`.

#### ISC-44.x deferral tracking (per Architect plan-reeval-1 START directive)

> Every "Coming in subsequent layers" deferral enumerated in a shipped layer becomes a tracked `ISC-44.<tab>.<deferral>` so the partial-parity surface is countable. Three terminal statuses: `DEFERRED` (will be ported), `DROPPED` (no browser equivalent — won't be ported), `MISSING` (must be added, blocks ideal state). See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Adopted `ISC-44.<tab>.<deferral>` tracking convention").

- [x] ISC-44.general.wakatime: Settings General tab's wakatime status + API-key validation surfaced via `/api/wakatime/*` REST routes. **CLOSED (server-half) 2026-06-07** on branch `w2-wakatime-server-port`. Server-side `WakaTimeManager` ported to `src/server/wakatime-manager.ts` (no `electron` import, no `src/main/utils/*` imports). Additive REST routes added in `src/main/web-server/routes/apiRoutes.ts` (`GET /api/wakatime/status` mirrors `wakatime:checkCli` IPC; `POST /api/wakatime/validate-key` mirrors `wakatime:validateApiKey` IPC). `WakaTimeProvider` interface + `registerWakatimeProvider()` / `getWakatimeProvider()` lazy registry follows the SettingsProvider pattern from L3.1. Headless server wires the manager + provider in `src/server/index.ts` before `WebServer.start()`. webFull-side hook (`useWakaTimeStatus()` reading the routes from `GeneralTab.tsx`, replacing the "Coming in subsequent layers" panel entry) is the next follow-on; see Decisions 2026-06-07 ("W2 — WakaTime server-side port shipped"). The renderer-side `src/main/wakatime-manager.ts` and `src/main/ipc/handlers/wakatime.ts` are NOT touched — Electron continues using IPC; both stacks can run side-by-side because the `~/.wakatime/` binary cache and `~/.wakatime.cfg` config file are the cross-mode contract.
- [ ] ISC-44.general.sync: storage location + custom path + folder picker via `/api/sync/*`. Currently DEFERRED.
- [x] ISC-44.general.stats: Settings General tab's stats DB size + clear-old-data + earliest-timestamp surfaced via `/api/stats/*` REST routes. **CLOSED (server-half) 2026-06-08** on branch `w2-stats-server-port`. Server-side `StatsManager` ported to `src/server/stats-manager.ts` (no `electron` import, no `src/main/utils/*` imports, no `src/main/stats/` imports — fully self-contained mirror of the schema + migration runner + read-side CRUD + `clearOldData`). Five additive REST routes added in `src/main/web-server/routes/apiRoutes.ts`: `GET /api/stats/summary` (dbSize + earliestTimestamp + counts), `POST /api/stats/clear-old-data` (bulk delete past cutoff), `GET /api/stats/aggregation` (full dashboard aggregate), `GET /api/stats/query-events` (raw query events feed), `GET /api/stats/session-lifecycle` (session creation/closure events). `StatsProvider` interface + `registerStatsProvider()` / `getStatsProvider()` lazy registry follows the WakaTimeProvider pattern from W2-wakatime — no fallback default, routes 503 when no provider is registered (Electron path continues using `stats:*` IPC). Headless server wires the manager + provider in `src/server/index.ts` before `WebServer.start()`. webFull-side hook (`useStatsSummary()` reading the routes from `GeneralTab.tsx`, replacing the "Coming in subsequent layers" panel entry for stats) is the next follow-on. The renderer-side `src/main/ipc/handlers/stats.ts` and `src/main/stats/*` are NOT touched — Electron continues using IPC; both stacks can run side-by-side because the on-disk `stats.db` file is the cross-mode contract.
- [ ] ISC-44.general.shells: shells:detect + custom shell path + args + env-var editor. Currently DEFERRED (local-machine concept — server's machine may not match client's; design call needed).
- [ ] ISC-44.general.power: power.setEnabled (sleep prevention). Currently DROPPED (Electron-only; no browser equivalent).
- [ ] ISC-44.general.gpu_acceleration: GPU acceleration toggle. Currently DROPPED (Electron renderer setting).
- [ ] ISC-44.general.shell_open_path: shell.openPath ("open in Finder"). Currently DROPPED (no browser equivalent).
- [x] ISC-44.display.font_family: Settings Display tab's fontFamily picker surfaced via `GET /api/fonts/detected` REST route. **CLOSED (server-half) 2026-06-08** on branch `w2-fonts-server-port`. Server-side `FontsManager` ported to `src/server/fonts-manager.ts` (no `electron` import, no `src/main/utils/*` imports — fully self-contained mirror of the `fonts:detect` IPC handler at `src/main/ipc/handlers/system.ts` line ~120). One additive REST route added in `src/main/web-server/routes/apiRoutes.ts` (`GET /api/fonts/detected` — wraps the IPC's bare `string[]` reply in a `{ fonts, timestamp }` envelope for parity with the rest of `/api/*`). `FontsProvider` interface + `registerFontsProvider()` / `getFontsProvider()` lazy registry follows the WakaTimeProvider / StatsProvider pattern from prior W2 ports — no fallback default, route 503s when no provider is registered (Electron path continues using `fonts:detect` IPC). Headless server wires the manager + provider in `src/server/index.ts` before `WebServer.start()`. Stateless manager — no DB handle, no network egress, no SIGINT/SIGTERM hook needed; each `detectFonts()` call shells out fresh to `fc-list`. webFull-side hook (`useDetectedFonts()` reading the route from `DisplayTab.tsx`, replacing the "Coming in subsequent layers" panel entry for fontFamily picker) is the next follow-on. The renderer-side `src/main/ipc/handlers/system.ts` is NOT touched — Electron continues using IPC; both stacks can run side-by-side because the on-disk `fc-list` binary is the cross-mode contract. The "custom-font management" sub-deferral (font file upload + storage) is its own follow-on and remains open under a future ISC-44.display.custom_font_management entry — flagged here as "client-half DEFERRED" because it requires a new file-upload surface that the renderer side doesn't have either.
- [ ] ISC-44.display.window_chrome: useNativeTitleBar + autoHideMenuBar. Currently DROPPED (Electron BrowserWindow chrome).
- [ ] ISC-44.display.bionify_info_modal: bionify info modal. Currently DEFERRED (non-essential).
- [x] ISC-44.global.settings_broadcast: ISC-14 (CLOSED 2026-06-08) — `settings_changed` WS broadcast on server-side mutation so concurrent browsers stay in sync without reload. Was MISSING; shipped on `w2-isc14-settings-broadcast` (plan-reeval-1 N2 closure). Fan-out frame `{type:'settings_changed', changedKeys, newValues, timestamp}` emitted by headless server on every successful PATCH /api/settings; webFull `useSettings()` subscribes via module-level event bus and merges newValues into local state. Last-writer-wins per ISA Principle 2. See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("ISC-44.global.settings_broadcast shipped").
- [x] ISC-44.layer-4.1.session*list_lifted: Left Bar (SessionList) lifted from `src/renderer/components/SessionList/SessionList.tsx` (1247 LOC) to `src/webFull/components/SessionList.tsx`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `layer-4.1-session-list`. webFull now renders the agent list, supports click-to-switch via `onSelectSession`, paints state-color (idle/busy/error/connecting) via the lifted `<StatusDot>` Badge, renders groups with collapse/expand, and shows the Bookmarks section. Parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/SessionList.parity.test.ts` ships 9 stories (6 happy / 3 negative) using only the allowed assertion verbs. Wired into `src/webFull/mobile/App.tsx` via a thin `DesktopSidebar` adapter that derives `sessionsByGroup` from `useMobileSessionManagement().sessions` and renders the bar only on `!isSmallScreen` (mobile keeps `SessionPillBar`). 0 IPC namespaces touched; 0 `src/main/` touches; 0 `src/web/` touches; 0 `src/renderer/` touches — server-side `/api/sessions` + `sessions*\*` WS frames already existed from the original mobile-remote-control surface. See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Layer 4.1 — SessionList Left Bar shipped"). Deferrals from the renderer surface tracked as sub-ISCs below.

- [ ] ISC-44.layer-4.1.live_overlay: LIVE toggle + tunnel UI + persistent web link controls in sidebar header. Currently DEFERRED (the entire LIVE-overlay surface is meaningful for the Electron host that owns the local tunnel; for webFull running ON the tunnel, the surface needs a redesign — DROPPED candidate pending Decision).

- [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.error_boundary: `ErrorBoundary` (renderer `src/renderer/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx`, 163 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per pre-flight grep — `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` returned empty / exit 1) lifted verbatim into `src/webFull/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/ErrorBoundary.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-error-boundary` (leaf-parade lift wave — React class component that catches errors in its child tree via `componentDidCatch` + `getDerivedStateFromError`). Two import-path adapts: `@sentry/electron/renderer` → `../utils/sentry` (webFull's lazy `@sentry/browser` wrapper at `src/webFull/utils/sentry.ts`, ships the same `captureException(err, context?)` signature — same swap the L2.5 `QRCode` lift exercised); `../utils/logger` swaps the exported binding `logger` → `webLogger` (path string identical between renderer and webFull; both export an `error(message, context?, data?)` method with the same signature, so the call site is unchanged modulo the renamed import). `window.location.reload()` in `handleReload` is browser-standard — no adaptation needed. `lucide-react` icons (`AlertTriangle`, `RefreshCw`, `Home`) are already webFull-tree deps. Sentry call site was slightly normalized: the renderer source wraps its context payload in `{ extra: { componentStack: ... } }` per the `@sentry/electron/renderer` `CaptureContext` shape, but webFull's `captureException(err, context?: Record<string, unknown>)` takes a flat context map and folds it into Sentry's `extra` internally — the lift passes `{ componentStack: errorInfo.componentStack }` directly to match the webFull signature. Behavior is identical (`componentStack` lands under `extra` in both targets). Negative-path stories pin: children-pass-through with no error card chrome when `hasError=false`; Error Details block omission when `state.error` is null (the source's `{this.state.error && (...)}` guard); Component Stack Trace omission when `state.errorInfo` is null (matches the brief moment between `getDerivedStateFromError` and `componentDidCatch`); default-card suppression when `fallbackComponent` is supplied (header + button row both absent); and a no-IPC / no-WS / no-notification lifecycle pin on pure render. 0 IPC namespaces touched. 0 Electron-only APIs touched. 0 `src/main/` / `src/web/` / `src/renderer/` / `src/server/` touches. - [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.agent_error: `AgentErrorModal` (renderer `src/renderer/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx`, 264 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per audit item #6) lifted verbatim into `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-agent-error` (leaf-parade lift wave). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer"` against the renderer source returned empty (exit 1) — confirms the audit's 0-IPC + 0-Electron-API classification. Transitive deps audited: `Modal` is the L2.1-lifted webFull primitive; `lucide-react` icons have no Electron surface; `CollapsibleJsonViewer` (`src/renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx`, 303 LOC) has one impure import — `safeClipboardWrite` from `src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts` — which routes through `navigator.clipboard.writeText` only. The `window.maestro.shell.copyImageToClipboard` surface in `clipboard.ts` is exclusively inside `safeClipboardWriteImage`, a sibling function `CollapsibleJsonViewer` does NOT call (verified: only `safeClipboardWrite` is imported). Therefore the entire dependency chain is browser-safe and `CollapsibleJsonViewer` is pulled directly from the renderer by relative path (`../../renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer`) per the L2.5 precedent of importing pure leaves rather than duplicating into `src/webFull/` (audit risk A: silent-drift avoidance). Import-path adapts (matching the L2.5 precedent): `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`; `AgentError` + `AgentErrorType` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/types'` directly (both shapes already live in `src/shared/types.ts` and the renderer aggregator only re-exports them — routing through `src/shared/` is more direct and avoids the renderer-aggregator dependency entirely); `MODAL_PRIORITIES` resolves via the existing `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` re-export shim (uses `MODAL_PRIORITIES.AGENT_ERROR` = 1010 — same priority as renderer source). Composes the L2.1 `Modal` primitive directly with `width={hasJsonDetails && showJsonDetails ? 600 : 480}` + `zIndex={10001}` + `showCloseButton={dismissible}` + `headerIcon` + `initialFocusRef={primaryButtonRef}` (matches renderer source verbatim); no `ModalFooter` — the action surface is a vertical column of recovery-action buttons plus a separate optional Dismiss row, neither of which fits the two-button confirm/cancel idiom. Threads `theme` as a prop per the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 convention. Parity catalog ships 10 stories total (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: auth_expired title chrome rendering, agent+session context line rendering, recovery-action button column with primary+secondary action rendering, Dismiss row rendering when dismissible=true, JSON-details toggle rendering when parsedJson present; negative paths cover agent/session context line omitted when neither name supplied, JSON toggle omitted when parsedJson undefined, Dismiss row omitted when dismissible=false, fallback "Error" title for unknown type, and Escape closes via layer stack onClose=onDismiss. The lift carries: a constants block matching the renderer defaults (`DEFAULT_BIONIFY_REST_OPACITY = 0.65`, `DEFAULT_BIONIFY_INTENSITY = 1`), `resolveBionifyRestOpacity` (pure clamp helper), `getBionifyReadingModeStylesCss` (pure CSS-string generator — byte-equivalent to the renderer's `getBionifyReadingModeStyles` for the call shape used by `generateTerminalProseStyles`), and `generateTerminalProseStyles` itself (verbatim CSS template from the renderer source line 833+). The lift OMITS: the React-side `BionifyText` / `BionifyTextBlock` components, the style-injection side-effect, algorithm-parsing for runtime config, and all other `generate*ProseStyles` / `createMarkdownComponents` functions. **Parity guarantee:** the CSS string this file emits MUST match the renderer's output byte-for-byte for the same `(theme, scopeSelector)` inputs. If a future webFull port needs more of the markdown-config surface, the right move is a second surgical extract — NOT a full module lift — so the Electron-only deps don't leak. **Utility test (`src/webFull/utils/terminalProseStyles.test.ts`, 5 vitest cases — exceeds the brief's ≥3 floor):** verifies non-empty CSS string scoped to the given selector + `.prose`, theme-color emission for headings (h1=accent, h2=success, h3=warning) + code backgrounds (`bgSidebar`) + accent-with-underline links, inlined Bionify reading-mode rules with the dark-theme default `--bionify-rest-opacity` of 0.65, the light-theme rest-opacity shift to 0.73 (via `resolveBionifyRestOpacity` baseOpacity branch), and a scoping-pin that every emitted rule selector begins with the provided scope prefix. 5/5 pass. **Cross-fork debt drawdown:** with the three util lifts on this branch (text_processing_util + clipboard_util + terminal_prose_styles_util) + the already-merged participant_colors_util and markdown_renderer lifts, `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` now has ZERO cross-fork `renderer/` imports remaining (down from 6 at the original `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift). `grep 'renderer/' src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` returns 5 hits, all in the header comment block documenting the original lift context; `grep -E "^import.*renderer/|from ['\"].*renderer/" src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` returns empty. The GCM cross-fork debt is fully drained. Renderer-side consumers are UNTOUCHED — `markdownConfig.ts` and `bionifyReadingMode.tsx` stay canonical in `src/renderer/utils/`.

- [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.git_status_widget: `GitStatusWidget` (renderer `src/renderer/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx`, 244 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per pre-flight grep) lifted into `src/webFull/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/GitStatusWidget.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-git-status-widget` (leaf-parade lift wave, header widget). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The widget itself touches none of the banned surface. **One adapt decision worth naming (follows established precedent):** the renderer source self-sources git-status data from two focused contexts via `useGitFileStatus()` + `useGitDetail()`. The provider behind those contexts (`GitStatusProvider` in `src/renderer/contexts/GitStatusContext.tsx`) is built on `useGitStatusPolling`, which calls `window.maestro.git.getStatus(...)` at module-instantiation — lifting the context as-is would drag the entire git-status polling hook + the IPC site through the webFull bundle entry point (out of scope per the brief's "needs a server-side route which is out of scope" guard). Matching webFull pattern (per `AppOverlays` and `SessionList` L4.1 precedents): **promote the self-sourced values to props.** Two new inputs (`fileCount: number`, `fileDetails?: GitFileDetails`) replace `getFileCount(sessionId)` and `getFileDetails(sessionId)`. The widget contract no longer carries `sessionId` (the renderer source uses it only to key into the two hooks; with the hooks gone, there is no key). The host (a downstream layer-wiring pass that ports the git-status substrate as a REST + WS surface) decides where those values come from — a future webFull `useGitFileStatus()` hook reading `/api/git/status`, a global store, or prop-drilling from the App root. **Type-resolution adapts (matching the L2.5 precedent):** `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap). `GitFileChange` is NOT pulled from `'../contexts/GitStatusContext'` (which re-exports it from `useGitStatusPolling`) — instead the lifted module defines it locally (5 primitive fields: `path`, `status`, `additions`, `deletions`, `modified`). A new `GitFileDetails` aggregate captures the shape the renderer hook's `getFileDetails(sessionId)` returns (`{ fileChanges?, totalAdditions, totalDeletions, modifiedCount }`); the renderer declares this shape inline inside `GitDetailContextValue`, lifting it to a named type here keeps the prop contract greppable. Matches the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` / `DeleteWorktreeModal` precedent of pulling only the specific data shape each lifted module consumes, rather than copying the entire renderer aggregator into `src/shared/` (which would create the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against). `lucide-react` icons (`GitBranch`, `Plus`, `Minus`, `FileEdit`, `FileDiff`, `History`) kept verbatim — already a webFull-tree dep. - [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.template_autocomplete_dropdown: `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown` (renderer `src/renderer/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx`, 108 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per pre-flight grep) lifted verbatim into `src/webFull/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-silhouette-and-autocomplete` (leaf-parade lift wave, paired with `MaestroSilhouette` in one semantic atomic commit per the brief). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component is a `forwardRef<HTMLDivElement>` presentational dropdown that renders the absolute-positioned template-variable picker used by both the AI tab prompt composer (`AgentPromptComposerModal`) and the Auto Run document editor. Behavior is gated entirely on the `state` prop: returns `null` when `!state.isOpen` OR `state.filteredVariables.length === 0`; when rendered, emits a scrollable list of rows (each carrying `data-index={index}`, a `<code>` chip with the variable name, and a `<span>` with the description) plus a footer with three `<kbd>` chips (↑↓ navigate, Tab select, Esc close). Selection state lives entirely in the prop bag — the host owns the autocomplete reducer; this component is pure render. All side effects are delivered via the `onSelect(variable)` callback the host wires; hover effects directly mutate `currentTarget.style.backgroundColor` to preserve the renderer's exact behavior (no setState on hover). Negative-path stories pin the two halves of the `!state.isOpen || filteredVariables.length === 0` early-return (closed-but-non-empty AND open-but-empty cases both suppress the row + footer surface) plus the no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin on mount → hover → click. Renderer-side consumers (the AI tab `AgentPromptComposerModal` and the Auto Run document editor) are NOT touched — feature wiring into the webFull tree is a downstream-layer concern. - [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.app_overlays: `AppOverlays` (renderer `src/renderer/components/AppOverlays.tsx`, 129 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per pre-flight grep) lifted into `src/webFull/components/AppOverlays.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/AppOverlays.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-app-overlays` (leaf-parade lift wave, mid-size dispatcher leaf). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/AppOverlays.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The dispatcher itself touches none of the banned surface. **Two adapt decisions worth naming (both follow established precedent):** (1) **Store self-source stripped → promoted to props.** The renderer source uses the "Tier 1A" self-source pattern, reaching into `useModalStore` for three modal-data values (`standingOvationData`, `firstRunCelebrationData`, `keyboardMasteryData`) plus `useSettingsStore` for `shortcuts` + `disableConfetti`. Those two stores are renderer-only architecture as of this lift — `src/renderer/stores/settingsStore.ts` carries 20+ `window.maestro.settings.set` callsites and there is no `src/webFull/stores/` directory yet. Lifting the stores would explode this leaf into a multi-file wave that pulls in the entire IPC-persisted settings layer (and the modal-registry store with it). The matching webFull pattern: promote the self-sourced values to props (`standingOvationData`, `firstRunCelebrationData`, `pendingKeyboardMasteryLevel`). The host decides whether those values come from a future webFull-side modal store, REST-backed `useSettings()`, or prop drilling at the App root. This matches the L4.1 `SessionList` precedent of stripping renderer-specific store hooks at the lift boundary and letting the consumer wire the data source. (2) **Overlay children passed as render-prop slots, not imported.** The renderer dispatcher imports `StandingOvationOverlay`, `FirstRunCelebration`, and `KeyboardMasteryCelebration` directly. Of those three, only `FirstRunCelebration` is in webFull (lifted in `leaf-first-run-celebration` @ `fd9bc3cf9`). The other two are not yet lifted. Importing them from `'../../renderer/components/...'` was rejected for two reasons: `StandingOvationOverlay` carries a `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` callsite (pre-flight grep confirmed 1 hit), and cross-fork imports are the audit-risk-A silent-drift surface this fork-hygiene rule exists to prevent. Instead, the three overlays become render-prop `ReactNode` slots (`standingOvationSlot`, `firstRunCelebrationSlot`, `keyboardMasterySlot`). The dispatcher becomes a pure render-gate: when the data prop is non-null, render the matching slot; otherwise render nothing. The gate logic — the actual lift surface — is verbatim from the renderer source, including the render order (FirstRunCelebration → KeyboardMastery → StandingOvation). When the two unlifted overlays land in future leaf parades, the host wiring layer can keep the render-slot pattern (the dispatcher stays decoupled) or inline the three component imports at the host call site — either choice is host-local and the dispatcher contract is stable. **Import-path adapts (two, both matching L2.5 precedent):** `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`; `ConductorBadge` from `'../constants/conductorBadges'` → `'../../renderer/constants/conductorBadges'` (the constants module is pure data with zero IPC, zero Electron API surface — matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` / `MarkdownRenderer` precedent of pulling non-divergent renderer modules directly by relative path rather than duplicating into `src/shared/`). Theme is accepted as a prop per the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 convention; the dispatcher itself does not render any theme-styled DOM but keeps the prop on the surface for host convenience. **Parity catalog (`src/webFull/components/AppOverlays.parity.test.ts`, 10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor; 8 catalog-shape vitest guards):** render-shape oriented (per the L2.5 SessionListItem / ToggleButtonGroup precedent — `hasElement` only since the dispatcher is a pure visibility gate with no internal interaction surface). Happy-path stories cover the first-run slot rendering when data is present, keyboard-mastery slot rendering when level is non-null, standing-ovation slot rendering when data is present, keyboard-mastery slot rendering at `level=0` (boundary pin — a future refactor that uses `if (level)` instead of `if (level !== null)` would suppress level=0 and fail this story), and all three slots rendering simultaneously when all three data gates fire (with the render-order assertion pinning FirstRunCelebration → KeyboardMastery → StandingOvation). Negative-path stories cover suppression when each data gate is null (slot supplied but data gate null does NOT render — the dispatcher is data-driven, not slot-driven), the all-three-null steady state (none of the three markers present), and a lifecycle no-IPC / no-WS pin. Includes a **render-shape-only guard** (asserts the catalog uses only `hasElement` / `hasText` — no interaction or wire-frame verbs since the slots own all click / keyboard semantics) and a **render-order pin** (verifies the all-three-slots story declares its markers in the canonical FirstRunCelebration → KeyboardMastery → StandingOvation order so a future refactor that flips the order accidentally would fail the suite). Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; passes the IPC-leakage guard. **Renderer-side consumers UNTOUCHED:** `src/renderer/App.tsx` continues to render the renderer `AppOverlays` as part of the Electron entrypoint. Feature wiring into the webFull tree is a downstream-layer concern — and it has additional prerequisites (a webFull-side modal store and/or REST-backed source for the three data gates; lifts of `StandingOvationOverlay` and `KeyboardMasteryCelebration`). See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `AppOverlays` lift").
- [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.shortcuts_help: `ShortcutsHelpModal` (renderer `src/renderer/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.tsx`, 216 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only API per audit item #5) lifted verbatim into `src/webFull/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-shortcuts-help` (leaf-parade lift wave). Pre-flight grep flagged a single transitive dependency surface: the renderer's `formatShortcutKeys` (`src/renderer/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts`) leans on `isMacOSPlatform()` from `src/renderer/utils/platformUtils.ts`, which reads `window.maestro.platform` (Electron preload bridge). In a browser host that returns `''` and `isMacOSPlatform()` returns false, which would always render the non-Mac key map (`Ctrl+Shift+K` instead of `⌘ ⇧ K`). The platform-correct shim already exists at `src/webFull/utils/platformUtils.ts` (user-agent sniff, mirror API). To keep `src/renderer/` read-only AND get the browser-correct rendering, the lift inlines a thin `formatShortcutKeysForBrowser` wrapper inside the webFull component that mirrors the renderer formatter's key maps verbatim and routes platform detection through `webFull/utils/platformUtils`. The renderer's `formatShortcutKeys` is left untouched. Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards pass (6/6). Tiny presentational primitive: renders a two-column swatch grid grouped by `mode` (dark / light) with Moon / Sun icons above each section heading, active swatch ringed in the current accent colour, click handler is a plain `(id) => void` callback. **Import-path adapts:** single swap — `Theme` and `ThemeId` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (L2.5 precedent; webFull has no `types/` aggregator that re-exports these). **Composition shape:** no Modal / ModalFooter / layer-stack / `useLayerStack` / `MODAL_PRIORITIES` / `formatShortcutKeys` — just `react` + `lucide-react` (`Moon`, `Sun`, already webFull-tree deps used by sibling L2.5 lifts) + the two pure types. **Theme access pattern:** kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, plus the rich `themes: Record<ThemeId, Theme>` map prop that lets the picker render any registered theme's swatch using that theme's own colour palette for the swatch preview strip. **Settings plumbing intentionally out-of-scope:** the `setActiveThemeId` callback is a plain function — the actual settings-store write + cross-window broadcast lives upstream of this component (renderer-side `setActiveTheme` → `window.maestro.settings.set` → settings-broadcast, already covered by `ISC-44.global.settings_broadcast`) and stays in the renderer / will be lifted in its own brief when the webFull host wires this primitive into a Settings panel. Threads `theme` as a prop per the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 convention. Composition shape: presentational JSON tree — pure render component with internal `useState`-driven expand/collapse + clipboard-copy affordance per node. No `Modal` / `ModalFooter` / layer-stack registration (this is not a modal). **Parity catalog (`src/webFull/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.parity.test.ts`, 12 stories: 6 happy + 6 negative — meets brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor; 8 catalog-shape vitest guards):** render-shape oriented per the ToggleButtonGroup / SessionListItem precedent (`hasElement` + `hasText` only — click semantics, hover-to-reveal-copy, and clipboard-write semantics belong to the future feature-consumer's catalog or to the browser-API contract, not the primitive's). Happy-path stories cover object root with `{`/`}` brackets + quoted-key rendering + string/number value rendering, array root with `[`/`]` brackets + numeric entry rendering, primitive value categories (string quoted, number bare, boolean literal, null literal), per-node Copy affordance (`button[title="Copy value"]`), `rootLabel` surfacing as a top-level quoted key, and string truncation with the literal `...` marker when length exceeds `maxStringLength`. Negative-path stories cover primitive root (no brackets, Copy affordance still present), empty object / empty array bracket rendering without children chevron, no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle guard pinning the presentational contract, the no-modal-no-banner structural pin (asserts no story targets `[role="dialog"]` or `[role="alert"]` directly — the `:not(:has(...))` exclusion idiom remains permitted), and `undefined` literal rendering. Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; passes the IPC-leakage guard, the render-shape-only guard (no interaction verbs), and the no-modal-no-banner structural pin. `AgentErrorModal`'s cross-fork import remains intact in this branch by design — the retargeting cleanup is the follow-up wave per the brief. Presentational tool-execution card that surfaces tool call details from OpenCode and Codex session messages. Default-collapsed view: a single horizontal pill with `ChevronRight` + `"Tool: <name>"` label chip + status icon + `"Show more"` button. Click or keyboard activation (Enter/Space) expands to a sticky header with `ChevronDown` + label chip + status icon + `"Collapse"` button, an Input section (collapsible JSON), a status row carrying optional `"Time: <timestamp>"` label + literal `"Status: <status>"` text, and an Output section (collapsible JSON). Both name-keys honoured by exported `getToolName` helper (Claude's `name` key + OpenCode's `tool` key) — heterogeneous session entries render correctly. Status icon mapping verbatim: `completed`/`success` → `CheckCircle2` themed-success-green, `running`/`pending` → `Loader2` spinning themed-warning, `error`/`failed` → `AlertCircle` themed-error-red, default → `CheckCircle2`. Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/ToolCallCard.tsx` → empty. The component is pure render — all side effects are owned internally by `useState` toggles (expanded/collapsed); no callbacks fire upward. One import-path adapt matching the L2.5 precedent: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator). **Type shapes kept inline:** `ToolState` and `ToolUseEntry` are session-message data shapes the renderer source itself defines inline (the renderer does NOT pull them from a shared aggregator). The lift keeps the same inline definitions — they are narrow data shapes the component reads directly off the session message, with the source-of-truth living in the OpenCode / Codex session parsers (`src/main/parsers/`). Matches the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` / `QueuedItemsList` precedent of pulling only the specific data shape each lifted module consumes rather than copying the entire renderer aggregator into `src/shared/` (silent-drift surface audit risk A). **Composition shape:** no Modal / ModalFooter / layer-stack registration — the card is an inline transcript artefact rendered between message bubbles. The internal `CollapsibleContent` helper is kept inline verbatim (a tiny JSON.stringify + line-truncate widget); it is NOT replaced by the sibling L2.5 `CollapsibleJsonViewer` lift (which carries a richer tree-render contract — the two coexist; the renderer source's own internal helper has different chrome and the brief is a verbatim lift, not a chrome-convergence pass). `lucide-react` icons (`ChevronDown`, `ChevronRight`, `Clock`, `CheckCircle2`, `Loader2`, `AlertCircle`) kept verbatim — already a webFull-tree dep. **Theme access pattern:** kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, consistent with every L2.x lift. Parity catalog ships 11 stories total (5 happy + 6 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor): happy paths cover collapsed pill with `"Tool: <name>"` chip + `"Show more"` button + `[role="button"]` keyboard-activation surface, expanded view with `"Collapse"` button + chip + `"Status: <status>"` + `"Time: <timestamp>"` rows, OpenCode `tool` key honoured (heterogeneous session entry shape), Input/Output section labels with `<pre>` blocks, and timestamp-omission case rendering status row without time row. Negative paths cover empty-`toolUse=[]` null-render via `body:not(:has(button))`, collapsed view excluding the `"Collapse"` affordance (`button:has-text("Collapse")` negation), `getToolName` falling back to `"unknown"` when both name-keys are absent, no-modal-no-banner structural pin (`body:not(:has([role="dialog"]))` + `body:not(:has([role="alert"]))`), no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin on mount → expand-click → collapse-click, and errored-status case still rendering the tool chip with `"Status: error"` row. Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; 7 catalog-shape vitest guards pass (7/7) including a presentational-contract pin asserting no story targets `[role="dialog"]` or `[role="alert"]` positively (the `:not(:has(...))` exclusion idiom remains permitted). Barrel export added at `src/webFull/components/index.ts` (`export { ToolCallCard, getToolName } from './ToolCallCard';`). Renderer-side consumers are NOT touched — feature wiring into the webFull tree (the AI tab transcript view, the group-chat transcript view) is a downstream-layer concern. `src/web/` + `src/renderer/` + `src/main/` + `src/server/` UNTOUCHED (`git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ src/server/ | wc -l` → 0). `npm run lint` clean. `npx vitest run src/webFull/components/ToolCallCard.parity.test.ts` → 7/7 catalog-shape tests passed. Not pushed per brief instruction — branch sits locally at `leaf-tool-call-card`, awaiting Trillium's merge. **Unblocks one of two `GroupChatInput` preconditions** per the leaf-parade audit #7 cited in the brief: `src/renderer/components/GroupChatInput.tsx` imports `QueuedItemsList` directly (line 32 of the renderer source) and renders it inline above its textarea (line 456). Landing this leaf reduces the `GroupChatInput` blocking-deps count from 2 → 1; when both blockers land, the `GroupChatInput` lift becomes a verbatim sibling lift with all imports resolving inside the webFull tree, dropping the cross-fork edge the L2.5 `GroupChatPanel` lift currently carries (`'../../renderer/components/GroupChatInput'`). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/QueuedItemsList.tsx` → empty (`NO_MODULE_LOAD_ELECTRON_REFS` sentinel returned). The component is a pure presentational view — all side effects are delivered via prop callbacks (`onRemoveQueuedItem`, `onReorderItems`); internal state is the per-tab dismissal-confirmation id, the `Set<string>` of expanded message ids, and the drag/drop index pair. One import-path adapt matching the L2.5 precedent: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator). **Type-shape adapt:** the renderer source imports `QueuedItem` from `'../types'` which carries 10 fields (`id`, `timestamp`, `tabId`, `type`, `text`, `images`, `command`, `commandArgs`, `commandDescription`, `tabName`, `readOnlyMode`). This view actually touches only 6 of them (`id`, `tabId`, `type`, `text`, `images`, `command`) — the others are read by sibling consumers (e.g. `ExecutionQueueIndicator` reads `tabName`; the queue-browser modal reads `commandArgs` / `commandDescription`; the dispatcher reads `timestamp` / `readOnlyMode`). The lift defines a narrow `QueuedItem` shape directly in the lifted module covering the 6 fields it actually reads. This matches the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` precedent of pulling only the specific data shape each lifted module consumes rather than copying the entire renderer aggregator into `src/shared/` (which would create the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against). The local shape is strictly narrower than the renderer's full `QueuedItem` so it remains a structural-subtype — when/if webFull's `SessionData` grows an `executionQueue` field over the WebSocket protocol carrying the full `QueuedItem`, callers can pass real items directly without changes here. **Composition shape:** no `Modal` / `ModalFooter` / layer-stack registration — the panel renders inline above the prompt input and gates its own ephemeral confirmation modal (a bare `fixed inset-0` overlay, not a `Modal` primitive — verbatim from the renderer source; future plumbing could re-port the confirmation onto the L2.1 `Modal` if the chrome ever converges, but that's out of scope per the verbatim-lift rule). HTML5 drag-and-drop reordering via the four-handler dance (`onDragStart`, `onDragOver`, `onDragEnd`, `onDragLeave`) preserved verbatim; drag is gated on `onReorderItems` presence AND `filteredQueue.length > 1`. `lucide-react` icons (`X`, `ChevronDown`, `ChevronUp`, `GripVertical`) kept verbatim — already a webFull-tree dep. **Theme access pattern:** kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, consistent with every L2.x lift. Parity catalog ships 12 stories total (6 happy + 6 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor): happy paths cover the QUEUED separator with literal "(<count>)" copy, per-item message and command text rendering, the Remove `[title="Remove from queue"]` affordance, the "Show all (N lines)" expand toggle for messages >200 chars, the plural "<N> images attached" indicator, and the confirmation-modal copy ("Remove Queued Message?" / "Cancel" / "Remove") when Remove is clicked; negative paths cover empty-queue null-render, `activeTabId` filter that excludes all items (null-render), suppression of the "Show all" toggle when message ≤200 chars, suppression of the "attached" indicator when no images, the no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin, and the singular "1 image attached" boundary case (a future refactor using `>= 1` instead of `> 1` for the plural gate would silently break grammar). Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards pass (6/6) including a presentational-contract pin asserting the catalog never drifts toward `[role="dialog"]` positive targets on the panel root (the panel is inline chrome, NOT a modal — the confirmation it gates is a separate ephemeral surface). Renderer-side consumers (`GroupChatInput`, `TerminalOutput`) are NOT touched — feature wiring into the webFull tree is a downstream-layer concern. When the second `GroupChatInput` blocking dep (per audit #7) lands, the `GroupChatInput` lift's sibling-import line will resolve to `./QueuedItemsList` inside the webFull tree. See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `QueuedItemsList` lift").

Second of the three overlays referenced in `AppOverlays.tsx`'s file header to land in webFull (after `FirstRunCelebration` @ `fd9bc3cf9`); `StandingOvationOverlay` remains deferred for a separate brief on account of its `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` callsite. Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component touches none of the banned surface; all input is via the prop bag (`theme`, `level`, `onClose`, optional `shortcuts`, optional `disableConfetti`) and all side effects are the `canvas-confetti` burst on mount + on-close, the layer-stack registration (`MODAL_PRIORITIES.KEYBOARD_MASTERY` = 1095, focusTrap: 'strict'), the `keydown` listener for Enter / Escape dismissal, and the `onClose()` callback the host wires. **Import-path adapts (seven, all matching L2.5 precedent):** `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap); `Shortcut` from `'../types'` → `'../../renderer/types'` directly (the interface lives in the renderer types barrel only — `src/renderer/types/index.ts` — and is not yet replicated to `src/shared/`; matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` / `GroupChatHeader` precedent of pulling specific types from the canonical renderer aggregator; `Shortcut` is a pure data shape with no transitive `window.maestro` references); `useLayerStack` resolves to the webFull-side context at `src/webFull/contexts/LayerStackContext.tsx` (lifted in L2.1); `MODAL_PRIORITIES` resolves via the webFull re-export at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (audit risk A non-divergent re-export); `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS` from `'../constants/keyboardMastery'` → `'../../renderer/constants/keyboardMastery'` (pure data — level definitions `{ id, name, threshold, description }`, zero IPC at module load — matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` precedent of pulling non-divergent renderer constants directly by relative path rather than duplicating into `src/shared/`); `DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS` from `'../constants/shortcuts'` → `'../../renderer/constants/shortcuts'` (same rationale, pure data); `isMacOSPlatform` resolves to the webFull-side shim at `src/webFull/utils/platformUtils.ts` (`navigator.userAgent`-based instead of the renderer's `window.maestro.platform` preload bridge). The component's local `formatShortcutKeys(keys: string[], isMac: boolean)` helper is preserved verbatim from the renderer source — it takes a `(keys, isMac)` signature and joins without a separator (e.g. `['Meta', '/']` → `'⌘/'`), which is a different signature from the webFull `shortcutFormatter` shim's `formatShortcutKeys(keys, separator?)`. Keeping the helper local preserves source fidelity (renderer uses this no-separator form intentionally for the shortcut hint copy "Press ⌘/ to see all shortcuts"). **Composition shape:** large celebration modal — does NOT compose the L2.1 `Modal` primitive directly because the renderer source builds bespoke DOM chrome (dark backdrop at z-index 99997, gradient header glow, animated bouncing icon, level-progress dot row, music-themed confetti palette with per-level intensity scaling — 50/100/200/300/500 particles for levels 0-4, gradient dismiss button, level-specific message swap between `Keyboard` + "Level Up!" for levels 0-3 and `Trophy` + "Keyboard Maestro!" for level 4). Confetti `zIndex` stays at 99998 (between backdrop and modal). Maestro variant (`level === 4`) fires an extra delayed 100-particle gold-star burst at 300ms after mount. All confetti calls honour `prefers-reduced-motion` AND the `disableConfetti` prop. All timeouts are tracked in `timeoutsRef` and cleared on unmount to avoid leaking timers. Layer-stack registration uses `MODAL_PRIORITIES.KEYBOARD_MASTERY` (1095, just below `STANDING_OVATION` at 1100) with `focusTrap: 'strict'` and routes Escape to `handleClose()`. Celebration-on-close pattern: clicking the dismiss button (or pressing Enter/Escape) sets `isClosing`, fires a second confetti burst, then calls `onClose()` after an 800ms animation delay. The Continue button label flips to "Onwards!" during the `isClosing` window — preserved verbatim from the renderer source. **Parity catalog (`src/webFull/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.parity.test.ts`, 10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative — meets brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards):** happy-path stories cover the standard "Level Up!" variation chrome (dialog with the canonical `aria-label="Keyboard Mastery Level Up"`, level name + description from `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS`, Continue button), the next-level encouragement copy "Keep using shortcuts to reach <next>" with dismiss hint, the level-progression dot row rendering, the Maestro variation at `level === 4` swapping title to "Keyboard Maestro!" + "the highest level" subhead + "You've mastered all keyboard shortcuts!" encouragement copy, and the level=0 boundary case (Beginner tier — pin against future refactors that use `if (level)` instead of explicit `level === 4`). Negative-path stories cover Continue button → unmounts the dialog after the 800ms close-animation, Escape key → same close path via layer-stack `onEscape`, backdrop click → close (with the card's `onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}` preserved so card-clicks DO NOT close), no "Keep using shortcuts to reach the next level" copy at Maestro (the next-level branch must NOT render at level 4), and no "Level Up!" title at Maestro (the standard branch must NOT render at level 4). Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; 6/6 in-suite catalog-shape vitest guards green. **Scope guards verified:** `src/web/` + `src/renderer/` + `src/main/` + `src/server/` untouched (`git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ src/server/ | wc -c` → 0). Renderer-side consumers (the `?` / `Meta+/` shortcut handler that surfaces the celebration when crossing a level boundary, and the `useModalStore` reducer that tracks `keyboardMasteryData`) are NOT touched — feature wiring into the webFull tree is a downstream-layer concern (consumer needs the level-transition source wired against the webFull modal-data prop drilling, which is part of the deferred `AppOverlays` host-wiring brief). See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `KeyboardMasteryCelebration` lift; unblocks `AppOverlays`'s `keyboardMasterySlot` deferral").
- [x] ISC-44.layer-2.5.lightbox_modal: `LightboxModal` (renderer `src/renderer/components/LightboxModal.tsx`, 256 LOC, 0 module-load IPC, 0 Electron-only module-load API per pre-flight grep `grep -n "window\.maestro\|window\.electron\|ipcRenderer\|window\.api" src/renderer/components/LightboxModal.tsx` → empty) lifted verbatim into `src/webFull/components/LightboxModal.tsx` with parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/LightboxModal.parity.test.ts`. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `leaf-lightbox-modal` (leaf-parade lift wave). Pure UI primitive composing the L2.1 `ConfirmModal` for the destructive delete-image confirmation and registering with the LayerStack at `MODAL_PRIORITIES.LIGHTBOX` so Escape-handling cascades correctly with parent overlays. **Import-path adapts** (matching the L2.5 precedent set by `DeleteAgentConfirmModal`, `CollapsibleJsonViewer`, and `QueuedItemsList`): `useLayerStack` from `'../contexts/LayerStackContext'` (now resolves to the webFull L2.1 LayerStack lift), `MODAL_PRIORITIES` from `'../constants/modalPriorities'` (webFull re-export shim at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` — non-divergent constants stay re-exported per Architect 2026-06-08 audit risk A), `ConfirmModal` from `'./ConfirmModal'` (webFull L2.1 primitive), `Theme` from `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator), `formatShortcutKeys` from `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` (webFull-side mirror of the renderer API), and `safeClipboardWriteImage` from `'../../renderer/utils/clipboard'` (re-import precedent set by `GroupChatMessages` for the sibling `safeClipboardWrite` text-only function). **Runtime-only Electron branch documented but out-of-scope for the parity contract:** `safeClipboardWriteImage` internally optional-chains `window.maestro?.shell?.copyImageToClipboard`; on webFull `window.maestro` is undefined and the implementation falls through to the browser `navigator.clipboard.write()` path via `fetch(dataUrl) → blob() → ClipboardItem`. That branch is library-internal to `clipboard.ts` and is NOT part of `LightboxModal`'s observable contract — the parity catalog asserts only the copy-button UX (icon swap + "Copied!" confirmation), not the underlying transport. **Composition shape:** mounts a full-bleed `<div role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-label="Image Lightbox">` overlay with `absolute inset-0 z-[100] bg-black/90`; renders the expanded image centred; renders left/right arrow buttons when `stagedImages.length > 1`; renders a top-right Copy button (always) and a top-right Delete button (gated on `onDelete` callback presence); renders a bottom info strip with the "Image X of Y" counter, the "← → to navigate" hint, the "Delete to remove" hint (when canDelete), and the "ESC to close" hint; composes `ConfirmModal` on top when the delete-confirmation gate is open. Keyboard handling: ArrowLeft/ArrowRight navigate, Delete/Backspace open the confirm modal (when canDelete), Cmd/Ctrl+C copies to clipboard, Escape routes through the LayerStack `onEscape` handler. **Default-theme fallback:** when no `theme` prop is supplied, the component constructs a Dracula-mode `Theme` literal inline (verbatim from renderer source) so `ConfirmModal` always has chroma to render against. **Theme access pattern:** keeps the renderer's optional `theme: Theme` prop convention. Parity catalog ships 8 stories total (4 happy + 4 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) with 6 catalog-shape vitest guards (happy floor, negative-per-happy floor, allowed-verbs, non-empty given/when/then, unique-names, IPC-leakage guard). Happy paths cover dialog chrome + image render with a single staged image, navigation arrow visibility + "Image X of Y" counter with multiple staged images, right-arrow advances counter, and Delete button visibility when `onDelete` is provided. Negative paths cover navigation-arrow suppression with a single staged image, Delete button suppression when `onDelete` is omitted, Escape-via-LayerStack closes the dialog, and Delete key opens the composed ConfirmModal without committing. Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary; the IPC-leakage guard pins the banned-target list (`window.maestro`, `shell.openpath`, `dialog.`, `tunnel.`, `ipcrenderer`). Renderer-side consumers (`GroupChatInput`, `TerminalOutput` image staging) are NOT touched — feature wiring into the webFull tree is a downstream-layer concern. `src/web/` + `src/renderer/` + `src/main/` untouched (additive lift only — barrel export added, no patches to upstream files). See Decisions 2026-06-08 ("Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `LightboxModal` lift").
- [x] ISC-44.layer-4.2.tab_switch_lifted: AI-tab navigation (TabBar) lifted from `src/webFull/mobile/TabBar.tsx` (719 LOC, originally a verbatim copy of `src/web/mobile/TabBar.tsx`) to `src/webFull/components/TabBar.tsx`, plus renderer-aligned keyboard shortcuts wired through a new `useTabKeyboardShortcuts` hook. **CLOSED 2026-06-08** on branch `layer-4.2-tab-switch`. The desktop oracle `src/renderer/components/TabBar.tsx` (2137 LOC) carries file-preview tabs, HTML5 drag-and-drop, merge-session, summarize-and-continue, gist publish, copy-context, export-html, mark-unread filter, close-others/left/right batches, and reopen-closed-tab — all out of scope for L4.2 (each enumerated as a DROPPED entry in the TabBar header + the parity catalog so the partial-parity surface stays countable per the ISC-44.<tab>.<deferral> convention). Keyboard shortcuts (new `src/webFull/hooks/useTabKeyboardShortcuts.ts`): Cmd+Shift+] / Cmd+Shift+[ for next/previous AI tab (wraps), Cmd+1..9 for jump-to-index, Cmd+0 for jump-to-last — matching `src/renderer/constants/shortcuts.ts` lines 58-59 + 183+ (`prevTab` / `nextTab` / `goToTab1..9` / `goToLastTab`). Browser-conflict caveat documented in the hook header + parity catalog: Cmd+Shift+[/] and Cmd+1..9 are bound to browser tab navigation in Chrome / Safari / Firefox on macOS in a regular browser tab; they work in PWA / standalone display mode (the intended deployment) and in the headless test harness. The hook calls `e.preventDefault()` defensively and is inert when any `<input>` / `<textarea>` / contenteditable is focused (renderer's `isInputFocused` guard mirrored). The existing `useMobileKeyboardHandler` Cmd+[/] (no Shift) navigation is kept additive — mobile muscle memory unchanged. Parity catalog at `src/webFull/components/TabBar.parity.test.ts` ships 14 stories total: 9 happy-path (tab row rendering with state attrs, click-to-select, close-button, new-tab, search, Cmd+Shift+] / Cmd+Shift+[ wrap, Cmd+digit index jump, Cmd+0 last-tab) + 5 negative-path (clicking active tab is idempotent, single-tab case hides bar, Cmd+digit out-of-range is no-op, shortcuts inert while typing, drag-reorder is intentionally absent) — exceeds the "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor; 7 vitest catalog-shape guards (happy floor, negative-per-happy floor, allowed-verbs, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard, browser-conflict flag guard, droppedFromWebFull-is-negative guard). Wire-up in `src/webFull/mobile/App.tsx`: one import-path adjustment (`from './TabBar'` → `from '../components/TabBar'`), one additive import (`useTabKeyboardShortcuts`), one additive hook call adjacent to the existing `useMobileKeyboardHandler` mount. The old `src/webFull/mobile/TabBar.tsx` is now a 13-line re-export shim that points at `'../components/TabBar'` so legacy imports keep resolving. **Scope guards verified:** `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ | wc -c` → 0 (fork-hygiene); `git diff main..HEAD -- src/renderer/ | wc -c` → 0 (read-only oracle); `git diff main..HEAD -- src/main/ | wc -c` → 0 (no new routes needed — existing `select_tab` / `new_tab` / `close_tab` / `rename_tab` WS frames from the original mobile-remote-control surface cover the wire). 0 IPC namespaces touched. Deferrals from the renderer surface tracked as sub-ISCs below.
