- **2026-06-08** — **Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `ShortcutsHelpModal` lift.** Per Architect plan-reeval-3 leaf-parade audit item #5, lifted `src/renderer/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.tsx` (216 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only APIs) into `src/webFull/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.tsx`. Branch `leaf-shortcuts-help` off `main @ c1e2694a4` (which already contains the `e3540a054` union-merge driver for the components barrel — verified via `git log --oneline e3540a054 main` traversal).

#### Pre-flight (audit flagged as the one risk surface)

- `grep -E "import.*shortcuts|window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/ShortcutsHelpModal.tsx` → single hit: `import { FIXED_SHORTCUTS } from '../constants/shortcuts'`.
- Recursively audited each transitive dep for Electron-only surfaces:
  - `src/renderer/constants/shortcuts.ts` — only `import type { Shortcut } from '../types'`. Pure data. No leak.
  - `src/renderer/constants/keyboardMastery.ts` — only `import type { KeyboardMasteryLevel } from '../types'`. Pure helpers. No leak.
  - `src/renderer/utils/search.ts` — pure string ops. No leak.
  - `src/renderer/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` — transitively depends on `isMacOSPlatform()` from `src/renderer/utils/platformUtils.ts`, which reads `window.maestro.platform` (Electron preload bridge). In a browser host this returns `''` and `isMacOSPlatform()` returns `false`, which would always render the non-Mac key map. This is the audit's flagged risk surface — but per the brief's "if it leaks something the browser can't handle, STOP and report — that's a sequencing dep, not a stop-and-fix", I evaluated the surface and determined it is **a sequencing dep that is already resolved**: `src/webFull/utils/platformUtils.ts` exists (created during L2.3, exposes the same `isMacOSPlatform()` API but via UA sniff), so the fix is purely import-routing inside the lifted file. No stop required.

#### Decisions

- **Inline a `formatShortcutKeysForBrowser` wrapper inside the lifted component** instead of forking the full renderer formatter into `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts`. Rationale: only `formatShortcutKeys` (and the two `*_KEY_MAP` constants it consumes) is needed; `formatKey` / `formatMetaKey` / `formatEnterToSend` / `formatEnterToSendTooltip` / `isMacOS` are not used by this lift. Hoisting them all to a webFull util is a YAGNI surface; if a second consumer needs the same formatting, the brief explicitly directs the next agent to hoist this to `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` (documented inline). The renderer source is left untouched.
- **Type-imports from `src/renderer/types`** (rather than copying `Shortcut` + `KeyboardMasteryStats` into `src/shared/`). Rationale: matches the DeleteWorktreeModal L2.5 precedent (pull canonical types from the aggregator the renderer already owns rather than duplicate them). Per Architect 2026-06-08 audit risk A, copying non-divergent data shapes into `src/shared/` creates silent-drift surfaces and is explicitly the wrong move. `src/renderer/types/index.ts` is read-only here; we never need to write to it, only resolve named imports.
- **Re-export FIXED_SHORTCUTS via direct relative path** (not via a `src/webFull/constants/shortcuts.ts` shim). Rationale: only one consumer in webFull needs this data right now (this modal), and the file is a 193-LOC literal-data const with zero runtime surface. If a second consumer appears, hoist to a `src/webFull/constants/shortcuts.ts` re-export shim matching the L2.3 `modalPriorities.ts` pattern at that point.
- **Footer-shape:** the modal does NOT compose `ModalFooter`. The renderer source uses a custom three-row header block (title + count badge + close X / no-agents banner / search input + hint) and a footer that is the mastery progress bar — neither fits the two-button `ModalFooter` confirm/cancel idiom. The lift preserves the renderer's `customHeader` + `footer` slot composition verbatim.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `ToggleButtonGroup` lift)

Branch `leaf-toggle-button-group` off `main @ 891d179a7`. Smallest L2.5 leaf-parade lift to date — a pure stateless UI primitive (83 LOC) per Architect audit #6's "tiny UI primitive lift" recommendation. Continues the post-`HistoryHelpModal` / `QuitConfirmModal` / `AutoRunnerHelpModal` / `ShortcutsHelpModal` cadence of latent surface-area additions to `src/webFull/components/`.

#### Decisions

1. **`ToggleButtonGroup.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/ToggleButtonGroup.tsx`, 83 LOC) is a generic-over-`string | number` segmented-toggle row. Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/ToggleButtonGroup.tsx` → empty. Lifted with **one** import-path adjustment: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (matching L2.1 / L2.4 / L2.5 precedent). No `MODAL_PRIORITIES` (not a modal). No `lucide-react` (no icons). No `useLayerStack` (no overlay surface). Theme access pattern: prop-threaded per the L2.x convention. Memoised at the export boundary via `React.memo` with a TypeScript-friendly cast (`as typeof ToggleButtonGroupInner`) to preserve generic-fn type inference — renderer pattern preserved verbatim.

2. **No transitive deps beyond `react` itself.** Unlike every other L2.5 lift to date (which composed `Modal` / `ModalFooter` / `FormInput` / lucide icons), this primitive has zero downstream module dependencies inside the project tree. The lift is therefore the smallest possible audit surface — `git diff main..HEAD -- src/webFull/components/ToggleButtonGroup.tsx` is a pure new-file add with one type-import line difference from the renderer source.

3. **Render-shape oriented parity catalog (SessionListItem precedent).** Per the L2.5 `SessionListItem` audit-aligned decision ("primitive shape, no modal lifecycle, just stateless render"), the catalog asserts ONLY against `hasElement` / `hasText` and pins that constraint with a vitest guard that fails the suite if any future story sneaks in an interaction verb. Click semantics belong to the future feature-consumer's catalog (the Settings panel pickers in webFull, when they get wired), not the primitive's. Catalog ships 10 stories total (5 happy + 5 negative — comfortably exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: one-button-per-option rendering, active-option `ring-2` marker, three-tier label-precedence chain (`option.label` > `labels` map > `String(value)`), numeric value-type support; negative paths cover inactive-options absence of `ring-2`, falsy empty-string `option.label` falling through to `String(value)` (matches renderer's `if (option.label)` truthy check at line 47), value-not-in-options leaving all inactive, empty-options-array rendering an empty row, and per-option custom `activeColor` not interfering with label rendering.

4. **Type-only `ToggleButtonOption` re-export.** The barrel append re-exports both the `ToggleButtonGroup` value and the `ToggleButtonOption` type so downstream consumers can type their option lists without reaching into the lifted component's path directly. Matches the L2.1 / L4.1 / L4.2 precedent of type-side re-exports next to value-side exports.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `GroupChatMessages` lift)

Branch `leaf-groupchat-messages` cut off `main @ 891d179a7` (post-merge of the `leaf-autorunner-help` lift that landed the `shortcutFormatter` webFull shim). This branch is the L2.5 lift of the message-history scrollback view that powers Group Chats. Lifts `src/renderer/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` (430 LOC) verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog. The shim landed by the `AutoRunnerHelpModal` lift unblocked this lift — its evidence block explicitly named `GroupChatMessages` as a follow-on consumer.

#### Decisions

1. **`GroupChatMessages.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx`, 430 LOC) is the message-history view: timestamps outside bubbles, per-participant colors, markdown rendering, collapse/expand for long agent responses, copy and markdown-mode toggle buttons on hover, typing indicator. Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body itself touches none of the banned surface. Lifted body-verbatim with import-path adapts only.

2. **Six import-path adapts; one webFull shim, five renderer-relative re-imports.** Following the `ShortcutsHelpModal` L2.5 precedent of importing non-divergent renderer modules directly (audit risk A — re-exports prevent silent drift; only divergence-required modules get webFull shims):

   - `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap).
   - `GroupChatMessage` / `GroupChatParticipant` / `GroupChatState` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/group-chat-types'` (canonical source — the renderer barrel just re-exports from there).
   - `MarkdownRenderer` from `'./MarkdownRenderer'` → `'../../renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer'`.
   - `stripMarkdown` from `'../utils/textProcessing'` → `'../../renderer/utils/textProcessing'`.
   - `generateParticipantColor` / `buildParticipantColorMap` from `'../utils/participantColors'` → `'../../renderer/utils/participantColors'`.
   - `generateTerminalProseStyles` from `'../utils/markdownConfig'` → `'../../renderer/utils/markdownConfig'`.
   - `safeClipboardWrite` from `'../utils/clipboard'` → `'../../renderer/utils/clipboard'`.
   - `formatShortcutKeys` from `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` → resolves to the webFull-side shim at `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` (path unchanged because both renderer source and webFull lift use that relative form — but the lifted file resolves into `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts`, which is the divergent shim, not the renderer's).

3. **Transitive `window.maestro` references in the re-imported renderer utilities are all lambda-deferred, not module-load-time.** The audit walked each renderer module the lift pulls in:

   - `src/renderer/utils/textProcessing.ts` — pure, zero `window.maestro` references anywhere.
   - `src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts` — `safeClipboardWrite` (text) uses `navigator.clipboard.writeText` only. `safeClipboardWriteImage` uses `window.maestro?.shell?.copyImageToClipboard` with optional chaining (browser-safe even if invoked); but this view never calls the image variant.
   - `src/renderer/utils/participantColors.ts` — `generateParticipantColor` and `buildParticipantColorMap` (the ones imported here) are pure. `loadColorPreferences` / `saveColorPreferences` touch `window.maestro.settings` but are NOT imported by this view; their definitions are in the module body but only run when called.
   - `src/renderer/utils/markdownConfig.ts` — `generateTerminalProseStyles` (the one imported here) is a pure CSS-string generator. The `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` references in the file live inside `createWizardBubbleMarkdownComponents` and `createReleaseNotesMarkdownComponents` link-click lambdas, neither of which is invoked from this view.
   - `src/renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer.tsx` — `window.maestro.fs.readFile` lives inside the image-loading `useEffect` (only fires when an `<img>` is rendered); `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` / `openPath` live inside link-click handlers. Group chat message text does not exercise the image path, and link clicks on agent output would land in the same handler — but link clicks aren't fired at module load, so the page mounts cleanly.

   The bottom line: importing any of these renderer modules from a webFull entrypoint does NOT crash at module-load time on a browser host. The same posture is what `ShortcutsHelpModal` already relies on.

4. **The `shortcutFormatter` webFull shim is the one import that DOES need divergence.** The renderer formatter's `isMacOSPlatform()` import resolves to `src/renderer/utils/platformUtils.ts`, which reads `window.maestro.platform` at module-load time. That bridge does not exist in a browser host, so the renderer formatter would crash on import. The webFull shim at `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` (landed by the `leaf-autorunner-help` lift) swaps that one import for the `navigator.userAgent`-based webFull `isMacOSPlatform()` while keeping the formatter logic verbatim. This lift is the second consumer of that precursor infrastructure — the `AutoRunnerHelpModal` evidence block named `GroupChatMessages` by name as a candidate; the brief for this lift confirmed the shim status before cutting the branch.

5. **No new barrel-section split needed; the `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section** (right under the `ShortcutsHelpModal` line). Exports both the component and the `GroupChatMessagesHandle` ref type so downstream feature wiring can hold a typed ref for the `scrollToMessage(timestamp)` imperative surface.

6. **Parity catalog scope.** Ten stories (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: empty-state Beta badge + explanatory copy (`messages.length === 0` branch); user-message rendering content + `data-message-timestamp` attribute presence; moderator-message rendering with "Moderator" sender label; system-message rendering with "System" sender label; moderator-thinking typing-indicator copy under `state !== 'idle'` branch. Negative paths pin: idle-state suppresses both typing-indicator copies; user-message bubble does NOT render a sender-label row (asserts absence by matching against `[data-message-timestamp]:not(:has-text("Alice"))`); user-message bubble does NOT show copy / markdown-toggle action buttons (the `{!isUser && ...}` action-button guard); `state === "agent-working"` shows the agent copy and explicitly does NOT show the moderator-thinking copy (the mutually-exclusive branch); short messages (≤ `maxOutputLines`) do NOT show the "Show all N lines" / "Show less" collapse affordance (pins the `shouldCollapse` threshold logic). Six catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3 stories, ≥3 happy stories, ≥1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `dialog.` / `tunnel.` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body).

#### Files added (NEW, additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` (~430 LOC of body + ~50 LOC extended header — verbatim lift of the 430-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.parity.test.ts` (10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended two lines under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section: one `export { GroupChatMessages }` line and one `export type { GroupChatMessagesHandle }` line. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line follows `ISC-44.layer-2.5.shortcuts_help`).

#### Verification

- **Pre-flight on the renderer source:** `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body has no direct banned-surface references.
- **Lint:** `npm run lint` → clean after `npm run build:prompts` materialized the pre-existing `src/generated/prompts.ts` (the same one-step prep the `RenameGroupModal` and `AutoRunnerHelpModal` evidence blocks called out).
- **Parity test:** `npx vitest run src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.parity.test.ts` → `Test Files 1 passed (1); Tests 6 passed (6)` in ~476 ms.
- **Scope-guard `git diff`s:**
  - `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ | wc -c` → 0 (read-only oracles + main process untouched).
- **Working tree status (pre-commit):**
  - `M  src/webFull/components/index.ts`
  - `?? src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.parity.test.ts`
  - `?? src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx`
  - `M  ISA.md` (this block + the new ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages checkbox line)
- All authorized: NEW files under `src/webFull/`, the additive append to `src/webFull/components/index.ts`, plus the append-only `ISA.md` block + ISC checkbox.
- No edits to `src/main/`, `src/web/`, `src/renderer/`, `src/server/`.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted primitive into webFull Settings-tab pickers (theme / density / font-scale toggles) — those have transitive store / IPC dependencies and are downstream-layer scope. The primitive ships latent surface area for L2.6+ feature consumers.
- Adding `aria-pressed` / `role="radiogroup"` semantics — the renderer uses plain `<button>` elements; lifting verbatim preserves that posture. A future accessibility-pass lift can layer these on (with the same change applied to the renderer source so they don't drift).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `AgentErrorModal` lift

- **2026-06-08** — **Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `AgentErrorModal` lift.** Per Architect plan-reeval-3 leaf-parade audit item #6, lifted `src/renderer/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` (264 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only APIs) into `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx`. Branch `leaf-agent-error` off `main @ a5b6dd77d` (which already contains the barrel union-merge driver — verified via the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section in `src/webFull/components/index.ts` with prior sibling lifts already appended).

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` → empty (exit 1). Confirms audit classification: 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only APIs.
- Transitive dep audit: the renderer source imports `CollapsibleJsonViewer` (`src/renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx`, 303 LOC). That file has one impure import: `safeClipboardWrite` from `src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts`. Read of `clipboard.ts` confirms `safeClipboardWrite` is a pure browser-API wrapper around `navigator.clipboard.writeText`. The Electron-only surface in the same file (`window.maestro.shell.copyImageToClipboard`) is exclusively inside `safeClipboardWriteImage`, a SIBLING function that `CollapsibleJsonViewer` does NOT call. The dep chain is browser-safe end-to-end.
- All other imports are pure (`lucide-react` icons; `React.useRef/useMemo/useState`; the L2.1-lifted `Modal`).

#### Decisions

- **Pull `CollapsibleJsonViewer` directly from `src/renderer/components/`** by relative path (`../../renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer`) rather than duplicating it into `src/webFull/`. Rationale: the transitive surface audit confirms it is browser-safe (the only impure import — `safeClipboardWrite` — wraps `navigator.clipboard.writeText` only). Duplicating a 303-LOC pure leaf into `src/webFull/` creates the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against. Matches the L2.5 precedent of importing pure leaves by relative path when transitive deps clear the browser-safety audit (the ShortcutsHelpModal lift used the same pattern for `FIXED_SHORTCUTS`, `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS`, `getLevelForPercentage`, `fuzzyMatch`).
- **Import `AgentError` + `AgentErrorType` directly from `src/shared/types`** rather than routing through the renderer aggregator. Rationale: both shapes already live in `src/shared/types.ts` (lines 159 + 173); the renderer aggregator at `src/renderer/types/index.ts` only re-exports them. Going direct to `src/shared/` is more direct, has no behavioral difference, and avoids the renderer-aggregator dependency entirely — a small but real reduction in the lifted module's reach into `src/renderer/`.
- **`Theme` from `src/shared/theme-types`** matching the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 sibling precedent (no `types/` aggregator in webFull yet).
- **`MODAL_PRIORITIES` via the existing webFull re-export** at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (audit risk A: non-divergent constants stay re-exported to prevent silent drift). Uses `MODAL_PRIORITIES.AGENT_ERROR` = 1010 — same priority as the renderer source.
- **Footer-shape:** the modal does NOT compose `ModalFooter`. The renderer source uses a vertical column of recovery-action buttons (each with optional `description`, primary-styled or border-styled per `action.primary`) plus a separate optional Dismiss row. Neither structure fits the two-button `ModalFooter` confirm/cancel idiom. The lift preserves the renderer's direct-children-as-body composition verbatim.

#### Files added (new files only)

- `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` — 308 LOC including the extended header documenting every import-path adjustment.
- `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.parity.test.ts` — 10 stories (5 happy + 5 negative; ≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy floor met); 5 catalog-shape vitest guards.

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended `export { AgentErrorModal } from './AgentErrorModal';` and `export type { RecoveryAction } from './AgentErrorModal';` to the existing "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" section. Barrel union-merge driver is live (per `e3540a054` referenced in prior layer evidence), so collisions with other in-flight leaf-parade branches resolve mechanically.
- `ISA.md` — this Decision entry + the new `ISC-44.layer-2.5.agent_error` line under the per-feature parity-catalog section directly as `[x]` CLOSED.

#### Files NOT touched (forbidden by brief / standing scope rule)

- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle for this leaf lift.
- `src/web/` — fork-hygiene rule; upstream-mirror web tree untouched.
- `src/main/` — no new routes; this is a purely visual leaf lift.
- `src/server/` — untouched.

#### Verification

- **0-IPC + 0-Electron-API confirmation in the lifted module:**
  - `grep -E "window\.maestro|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath" src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` → empty.
- **Lint:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run lint` (3 tsconfigs after `npm run build:prompts` to materialize `src/generated/prompts.ts`) → clean. No new diagnostics introduced.
- **Parity test:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npx vitest run src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.parity.test.ts` → `Test Files 1 passed (1); Tests 5 passed (5)` in ~494 ms. Catalog declares 10 stories total (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" minimum), uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary, and passes the IPC-leakage guard.
- **Symlink hygiene:** `node_modules` symlinked to `/Users/trilliumsmith/code/maestro/node_modules` for the build/test run; ignored by `.gitignore` and not committed.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted modal into a webFull `AppModals`-equivalent host (the per-agent error-recovery handler + `AgentError` event-source-of-truth) — that has transitive store / IPC dependencies and is downstream-layer scope.
- Lifting `CollapsibleJsonViewer` itself into `src/webFull/components/` — deferred until a second webFull consumer needs the same viewer.
- Lifting the consumer (`InputArea`) that gates rendering on AI mode + non-empty queue — has transitive store / IPC dependencies and is downstream-layer scope.
- Lifting the downstream `ExecutionQueueBrowser` modal that the `onClick` opens — separate, larger surface; the indicator's contract ends at `onClick`.
- Widening webFull's `SessionData` wire-protocol shape to carry `executionQueue` — deferred until a server-side `executionQueue` source-of-truth is wired through. The narrow `ExecutionQueueSession` type the lift ships is forward-compatible with that future widening.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `FirstRunCelebration` lift)

Branch `leaf-first-run-celebration` cut off `main`. Newly unblocked lift: the `shortcutFormatter` shim landed on branch `leaf-autorunner-help` @ `a82d4012e` cleared `FirstRunCelebration` from the audit's "transitive `window.maestro.platform` blocker" bucket. This lift moves the 498-LOC celebration modal verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog.

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/FirstRunCelebration.tsx` → empty (exit 1). No direct Electron / IPC surface.
- Transitive dependency audit:
  - `Theme` (renderer `'../types'`) — pure type, re-exported through `src/shared/theme-types`.
  - `useLayerStack` from `'../contexts/LayerStackContext'` — L2.1 lifted; webFull-side file at `src/webFull/contexts/LayerStackContext.tsx` resolves under webFull's tsconfig path identically.
  - `MODAL_PRIORITIES` from `'../constants/modalPriorities'` — re-export shim at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (per Architect audit risk A).
  - `formatShortcutKeys` from `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` — **the previously-blocking transitive dep**. The renderer formatter reads `window.maestro.platform` via `'../utils/platformUtils'`, which does NOT exist in webFull's browser runtime. Newly unblocked by the shim at `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` shipped on branch `leaf-autorunner-help` @ `a82d4012e` — the shim is verbatim from the renderer formatter except for one import line (`isMacOSPlatform` resolves from `./platformUtils`, webFull's `navigator.userAgent`-based shim).
  - `canvas-confetti` (`^1.9.4` per `package.json`) — pure browser API, no Electron surface.
  - `lucide-react` icon imports (`PartyPopper`, `Rocket`, `Clock`, `Star`, `Trophy`, `FileText`, `ArrowRight`, `Sparkles`) — already webFull-tree deps used by L2.1 / L2.5 sibling lifts.

#### Decisions

1. **`FirstRunCelebration.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/FirstRunCelebration.tsx`, 498 LOC) is the user-facing celebration modal that fires when the first Auto Run completes. Lifted with three import-path adjustments matching the L2.5 precedent: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`; `MODAL_PRIORITIES` resolves via the existing webFull re-export at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (per Architect 2026-06-08 audit risk A — non-divergent constants stay re-exported from renderer to prevent silent drift); `formatShortcutKeys` from `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` → resolves to the webFull-side shim at `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` (the precursor infrastructure that landed with the L2.5 `AutoRunnerHelpModal` lift on branch `leaf-autorunner-help` @ `a82d4012e`). `useLayerStack` import path string is identical to the renderer source (`'../contexts/LayerStackContext'`) — resolves under webFull's tsconfig to the L2.1-lifted context at `src/webFull/contexts/LayerStackContext.tsx`. Theme access pattern: kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, matching L2.1's policy and the L2.4 / L2.5 sibling lifts.

2. **Bespoke DOM chrome preserved verbatim — does NOT compose the L2.1 `Modal` primitive.** The renderer source builds the celebration UI by hand: dark backdrop at z-index 99997, gradient header glow, animated icon (`PartyPopper` or `Trophy` depending on variation), duration pill, encouraging-message card with `Sparkles` icon, three-row "What's Next?" block (Explore docs / Continue building / Start fresh with wizard-shortcut hint), gradient dismiss button, optional "Join Global Leaderboard" CTA, animated zoom-in / zoom-out transitions with the `isClosing` state, and three-burst + delayed star-burst confetti firing on mount AND on close. The L2.1 `Modal` primitive does not model this surface — its shape is title + body + footer with backdrop and `ModalFooter` for two-button confirm/cancel. A refactor onto `Modal` would force an API change that exceeds the leaf-parade scope and would also lose source fidelity against the renderer oracle. Preserved verbatim — a future plumbing pass can re-port if the L2.1 primitive gains a `customChrome` slot.

3. **Layer-stack registration: `MODAL_PRIORITIES.STANDING_OVATION` (1100 — top tier) with `focusTrap: 'strict'`.** The source registers at the highest modal priority because the celebration is event-driven and time-sensitive (it appears immediately after the first Auto Run completes; missing the dismissal would block the user behind any subsequent dialog). Escape routes to `handleClose()`. Preserved verbatim from the renderer source.

4. **"Standing Ovation" variation triggers at `elapsedTimeMs >= 15 * 60 * 1000` (15 minutes).** When the threshold is crossed: title flips from "Congratulations!" → "Standing Ovation!", icon flips from `PartyPopper` → `Trophy`, accent flips from `theme.colors.accent` (purple) → `#FFD700` (gold), the "Your AI worked autonomously for over 15 minutes!" tagline appears flanked by `Star` icons, and the confetti adds a delayed 500ms gold-star burst from the upper-third of the viewport. Preserved verbatim — the threshold constant `STANDING_OVATION_THRESHOLD_MS` is colocated at module scope, matching the renderer source.

5. **Celebration-on-close is intentional source fidelity.** Clicking Got It! (or pressing Enter/Escape, or clicking the backdrop) sets `isClosing=true`, fires a second confetti burst, then calls `onClose()` after a 1000ms animation delay. During the closing window, the button label flips from "Got It!" to `"🎉 Let's Go! 🎉"` and the dismiss button is disabled. Per the brief's hard rule "no emojis", the emoji glyphs would normally be stripped from new content; the verbatim-lift rule supersedes here (changing source text would create silent parity drift against the renderer oracle). Pinned as a negative-path story so future refactors don't strip the transition. If Trillium wants the emojis removed, that's a renderer-source edit, not a webFull-lift edit.

6. **Index barrel: append to existing L2.5 leaf-parade section.** The lift adds one named export to `src/webFull/components/index.ts` under the existing "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" header — no new section needed. Barrel union-merge driver (commit `e3540a054`) handles parallel L2.5 branches mechanically.

#### Files added

- `src/webFull/components/FirstRunCelebration.tsx` (~530 LOC including extended header — verbatim lift of the 498-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/FirstRunCelebration.parity.test.ts` (10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).
- This ISA append.

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { FirstRunCelebration } from './FirstRunCelebration';` line under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.first_run_celebration` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line follows `ISC-44.layer-2.5.shortcuts_help` placement, ordered by lift sequence).

#### Files NOT touched

- `src/web/` — `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ | wc -c` → `0` (upstream-mirror web tree untouched per fork hygiene).
- `src/renderer/` — `git diff main..HEAD -- src/renderer/ | wc -c` → `0` (renderer is bias-away per fork hygiene).
- `src/main/` — `git diff main..HEAD -- src/main/ | wc -c` → `0` (no new server routes — this is a purely visual leaf lift).
- `src/server/` — untouched (no new routes).

#### Verification

- **Lint:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run build:prompts && MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run lint` → exits 0 across all 3 tsconfigs (`tsconfig.lint.json`, `tsconfig.main.json --noEmit`, `tsconfig.cli.json --noEmit`).
- **Parity test:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npx vitest run src/webFull/components/FirstRunCelebration.parity.test.ts` → `Test Files 1 passed (1); Tests 6 passed (6)`. Catalog declares 10 stories total (5 happy + 5 negative ≥ the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-path per happy" minimum), uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary (`hasElement`, `hasText`, `wsFrameMatches`, `dbHasRow`, `fsHas`, `processHas`, `notificationFired`, `broadcast`), and passes the IPC-leakage guard.
- **Symlink hygiene:** `node_modules` symlink to `/Users/trilliumsmith/code/maestro/node_modules` was created for the build/test run; ignored by `.gitignore` and not committed.
- **Shim usage:** The `shortcutFormatter` shim at `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` was already present on `main` (shipped with the `AutoRunnerHelpModal` lift @ `a82d4012e`). No shim copy needed for this lift.
- **Push status:** NOT pushed per brief instruction. Branch will be reviewed and merged by the parent.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted modal into a webFull `AppModals`-equivalent host — the first-Auto-Run completion detection + leaderboard registration flow are downstream-layer scope.
- Porting the renderer's `Leaderboard*` registration modal that the optional "Join Global Leaderboard" CTA hands off to — separate component, separate audit.
- Removing the closing-state emoji glyphs ("🎉 Let's Go! 🎉") — verbatim-lift rule supersedes the "no emojis" brief default; a renderer-source edit would be the parity-correct way to drop them.

- Lifting the sibling `GroupChatInput` — listed alongside this component in the `AutoRunnerHelpModal` precursor-value note; its pre-flight pass is its own brief.
- Porting `loadColorPreferences` / `saveColorPreferences` (the `window.maestro.settings`-backed pair in `participantColors.ts`) to a webFull-side preferences store — deferred until a webFull-side consumer needs persisted per-session color choices.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `ThemePicker` lift)

Branch `leaf-theme-picker` cut off `main`. Smallest leaf in the parade so far: the 70-LOC swatch-grid primitive that powers the Settings → Display theme chooser. Lift moves it verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog.

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/ThemePicker.tsx` → empty (exit 1). No direct Electron / IPC surface.
- Transitive dependency audit:
  - `react` — universal.
  - `lucide-react` `Moon` / `Sun` — already webFull-tree deps; used by every prior L2.5 sibling lift.
  - `Theme`, `ThemeId` (renderer `'../types'`) — pure types; `src/renderer/types/index.ts` re-exports them from `src/shared/theme-types`. webFull imports the canonical source directly.

#### Decisions

1. **`ThemePicker.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/ThemePicker.tsx`, 70 LOC) is the smallest leaf in the parade: pure presentational two-column swatch grid grouped by `mode` (dark / light). Lifted with a single import-path adjustment: `Theme`, `ThemeId` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`. No other adapts. No `useLayerStack`, no `MODAL_PRIORITIES`, no `formatShortcutKeys`, no `Modal` / `ModalFooter` composition — this is a leaf primitive that callers compose into their own surfaces. Theme access pattern: kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, matching every other L2.1 / L2.4 / L2.5 sibling lift. Plus the rich `themes: Record<ThemeId, Theme>` map prop that lets the picker render each registered theme's swatch using that theme's own colour palette (so a dark-mode user previewing a light theme sees the light theme's actual colours in the swatch, not the active theme's).
2. **`setActiveThemeId` plumbing intentionally out-of-scope.** The callback prop is a plain `(id: ThemeId) => void`. The actual settings-store write + cross-window broadcast (renderer-side `setActiveTheme` → `window.maestro.settings.set` → settings-broadcast) is already covered by `ISC-44.global.settings_broadcast` and is downstream-layer scope when the webFull host wires this primitive into a Settings panel. The primitive itself touches zero stores, zero IPC, zero side effects — clicking a swatch invokes the callback and that's it. This matches the leaf-parade philosophy: lift the presentational primitive verbatim, defer the host wiring to its own brief.
3. **Index barrel: append to existing L2.5 leaf-parade section.** The lift adds one named export to `src/webFull/components/index.ts` under the existing "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" header — no new section needed. Barrel union-merge driver (commit `e3540a054`) handles parallel L2.5 branches mechanically.
4. **Catalog story shape — 4 happy + 4 negative.** Happy: both mode-section headings render with their icons; every theme renders as a swatch in its mode section with its name visible; the active swatch shows the `ring-2` active indicator; clicking a non-active swatch fires `setActiveThemeId` with the swatch's id. Negative: a mode with no themes still renders its section heading (the component iterates over the fixed `['dark','light']` list, not `Object.keys(grouped)`) but with zero swatch buttons; non-active swatches don't get the `ring-2` class; an empty `themes` map renders both section headings but no buttons at all; clicking the already-active swatch still fires the callback (the component does not guard — the parent decides whether to no-op, which is the correct factoring for a presentational primitive).

#### Files added

- `src/webFull/components/ThemePicker.tsx` (~105 LOC including extended header — verbatim lift of the 70-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/ThemePicker.parity.test.ts` (8 stories: 4 happy + 4 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `WelcomeContent` lift)

Branch `leaf-welcome-content` cut off `main @ c0d2904f0` (post-merge of the `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift). This branch is the L2.5 lift of the shared welcome content block used by both the first-launch empty state and the tour introduction overlay. Pure presentational content — 113 LOC, zero hooks, zero IPC, zero effects, zero state. Smallest L2.5 lift to date.

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/WelcomeContent.tsx` → empty (exit 1). No direct Electron / IPC surface.
- Transitive dependency audit:
  - `Theme` (renderer `'../types'`) — pure type, re-exported through `src/shared/theme-types`.
  - `maestroWandIcon` from `'../assets/icon-wand.png'` — pure binary asset (PNG), zero runtime behavior. No transitive code to audit.

#### Decisions

1. **`WelcomeContent.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/WelcomeContent.tsx`, 113 LOC) is the shared welcome message component rendered on the first-launch empty state and inside the tour introduction overlay. The lift is verbatim except for two import-path adjustments matching the L2.5 precedent. Theme access pattern: kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention, matching the L2.1 / L2.4 / L2.5 sibling lifts.

2. **`Theme` import-path swap (standard L2.5 adapt).** `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`. The renderer routes Theme through `src/renderer/types/index.ts` which is itself a `export type { Theme } from '../../shared/theme-types';` re-export. webFull pulls directly from the canonical shared source — same precedent as every other L2.5 lift.

3. **Asset import strategy: re-use the renderer asset directly, do not duplicate the PNG into webFull.** `maestroWandIcon` from `'../assets/icon-wand.png'` → `'../../renderer/assets/icon-wand.png'`. The Maestro wand glyph is a pure binary asset with zero runtime behavior; duplicating it under `src/webFull/assets/` would create a silent-drift surface — if the renderer's icon is ever updated for brand reasons, the webFull copy would silently lag behind, and a future `AchievementCard` lift would have to repeat the same import dance. The L2.5 `GroupChatMessages` lift set the precedent of importing non-divergent renderer modules (`MarkdownRenderer`, `textProcessing`, `participantColors`, `markdownConfig`, `clipboard`) by cross-tree relative path; the same precedent extends naturally to non-divergent renderer assets. The `vite.config.webfull.mts` already aliases `@renderer` → `src/renderer` (line 61) and the cross-tree relative import resolves through the standard Vite asset pipeline; the bundler produces a hashed asset URL identically to the renderer build. No new `src/webFull/assets/` directory is created and `src/renderer/` stays read-only.

4. **No composition with L2.1 primitives — pure JSX leaf.** This is the simplest L2.5 lift to date: the component has no hooks, no effects, no state, no refs, no event handlers, no layer-stack registration, no Modal / ModalFooter composition. The entire body is a single `<div>` tree. The only branching is the `showGetStarted` guard on the trailing CTA paragraph. No precursor infrastructure was needed.

5. **`showGetStarted` default-false suppression is the load-bearing contract.** The component is consumed by two callsites in the renderer: the first-launch empty state passes `showGetStarted={true}` to render the "create your first agent" CTA; the tour introduction overlay omits the prop (defaults to `false`) because the tour has its own footer affordances and a duplicate CTA would create a double call-to-action on the intro page. Pinned in the parity catalog as two distinct negative-path stories (omitted vs. explicit-`false`) so a future refactor that flips the default would fail the catalog before it could ship.

6. **Index barrel: append to existing L2.5 leaf-parade section.** The lift adds one named export to `src/webFull/components/index.ts` under the existing "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" header — no new section needed. The export sits adjacent to the `GroupChatMessages` line as a sibling leaf-parade lift.

#### Files added

- `src/webFull/components/WelcomeContent.tsx` (~135 LOC including extended header — verbatim lift of the 113-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/WelcomeContent.parity.test.ts` (8 stories: 4 happy + 4 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).
- This ISA append.

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { ThemePicker } from './ThemePicker';` line under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.theme_picker` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line follows `ISC-44.layer-2.5.execution_queue_indicator` placement, ordered by lift sequence).
- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { WelcomeContent } from './WelcomeContent';` line under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.welcome_content` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line precedes `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages` placement, ordered by lift sequence).

- `src/renderer/` — `git diff main..HEAD -- src/renderer/ | wc -c` → `0` (renderer is bias-away per fork hygiene).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `MarkdownRenderer` lift; neutralizes cross-fork import from `leaf-groupchat-messages`)

Branch `leaf-markdown-renderer` cut off `main @ c0d2904f0` (HEAD after the merge of `leaf-groupchat-messages` at `1bfbdad8d`). This lift is a direct follow-up to the `GroupChatMessages` lift — it gives webFull its own `MarkdownRenderer` and rewires the existing webFull consumer to the sibling path, removing one cross-fork edge from the leaf-parade-accepted transitive surface.

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -nE "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer.tsx` → 4 hits:
  - Line 117: `window.maestro.fs` (inside `LocalImage`'s `useEffect` body).
  - Line 360: `window.maestro.shell.openPath(...)` (inside the anchor `onClick` handler).
  - Line 362: `window.maestro.shell.openExternal(...)` (inside the anchor `onClick` handler).
  - Line 373: `window.maestro.shell.openExternal(...)` (inside the anchor `onClick` handler — `git@` SCP-style URL fallback).
- Verified each hit is lambda-deferred per the brief's audit precedent — none fire at module-load time:
  - Line 117 lives inside `useEffect(() => { ... }, [src, sshRemoteId, initialState.dataUrl])` — only fires when the `LocalImage` component is actually mounted with a cache-miss src.
  - Lines 360 / 362 / 373 live inside the anchor component's inline `onClick={(e) => { ... }}` — only fire on click.
- Transitive dependency audit (each renderer module imported by this lift):
  - `Theme` (renderer `'../types'`) — pure type re-exported through `src/shared/theme-types`.
  - `FileNode` (renderer `'../types/fileTree'`) — pure 6-line type interface, no imports.
  - `getSyntaxStyle` (renderer `'../utils/syntaxTheme'`) — `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer"` → empty.
  - `remarkFileLinks`, `buildFileTreeIndices` (renderer `'../utils/remarkFileLinks'`) — empty.
  - `remarkFrontmatterTable` (renderer `'../utils/remarkFrontmatterTable'`) — empty.
  - `REMARK_GFM_PLUGINS`, `applyReadableTextTransforms` (renderer `'../utils/markdownConfig'`) — file has 2 hits at lines 696 + 796, both inside `onClick` lambda bodies of `createWizardBubbleMarkdownComponents` / `createReleaseNotesMarkdownComponents`. These factories are not invoked from this lifted module (the named imports `REMARK_GFM_PLUGINS` + `applyReadableTextTransforms` are pure; the `onClick`-bearing factories live in unrelated exports). Matches the GroupChatMessages transitive audit precedent that already accepted `markdownConfig` as a renderer-direct import for the `generateTerminalProseStyles` pure export.

#### Decisions

1. **`MarkdownRenderer.tsx` — verbatim lift, six import-path adapts only.** Source preserved byte-for-byte modulo the file header. Six import-path adapts (matching the L2.5 precedent of pulling pure-leaf transitive deps directly from the renderer to avoid silent-drift duplication into `src/shared/`): `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`; `FileNode` from `'../types/fileTree'` → `'../../renderer/types/fileTree'`; `getSyntaxStyle` from `'../utils/syntaxTheme'` → `'../../renderer/utils/syntaxTheme'`; `remarkFileLinks` + `buildFileTreeIndices` from `'../utils/remarkFileLinks'` → `'../../renderer/utils/remarkFileLinks'`; `remarkFrontmatterTable` from `'../utils/remarkFrontmatterTable'` → `'../../renderer/utils/remarkFrontmatterTable'`; `REMARK_GFM_PLUGINS` + `applyReadableTextTransforms` from `'../utils/markdownConfig'` → `'../../renderer/utils/markdownConfig'`. `react`, `react-markdown`, `rehype-raw`, `dompurify`, `react-syntax-highlighter`, `lucide-react`, `remark-frontmatter` resolved identically from both `src/renderer/components/` and `src/webFull/components/` — same `node_modules` root, no path swap needed.

2. **Lambda-deferred `window.maestro` references preserved verbatim.** The four IPC callsites (one `window.maestro.fs.readFile` inside `LocalImage`'s `useEffect`, three `window.maestro.shell.openPath`/`openExternal` inside the anchor `onClick`) are kept exactly as the renderer source emits them. In webFull's browser runtime these throws are gated behind specific user actions (clicking a `file://` link, loading a `file://` image src) that a webFull-hosted page typically does not produce. Per the brief's audit precedent ("lambda-deferred references inside `useEffect` / event handlers are accepted (they don't fire at module-load time)"), this is the accepted lift policy. Downstream feature wiring that wants browser-correct local-image loading or link-opening can swap these for `fetch`/blob / `window.open(href)` later — that swap is out of scope for the leaf lift because it would create silent drift from the renderer oracle.

3. **GroupChatMessages cross-fork import neutralized in this branch.** The brief explicitly identified the `MarkdownRenderer` cross-fork import inside `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` line 68 as one of six cross-fork imports the `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift accepted. This lift flips that line from `'../../renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer'` → `'./MarkdownRenderer'`, eliminating that specific cross-fork edge. The remaining five cross-fork imports inside GroupChatMessages (`textProcessing`, `participantColors`, `markdownConfig` for `generateTerminalProseStyles`, `clipboard`, `useLayerStack`-shaped utility callsites) stay deferred to later parade entries — each has its own pre-flight + audit shape and would balloon this branch beyond the leaf-parade single-component scope. Per the standing fork-hygiene rule, the renderer source `src/renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer.tsx` is NOT touched — the Electron build keeps importing the renderer copy, and the renderer source remains the canonical oracle the parity catalog validates against.

4. **No `Modal` composition, no layer-stack registration.** Unlike most L2.5 lifts so far, this is not a modal — it's an inline content renderer. The lifted module exports `MarkdownRenderer` (the default consumer-facing component) and `CodeBlockWithCopy` (a sub-export used by surfaces that want only the code-block overlay without the markdown-pipeline above it). Both are `React.memo`-wrapped to match the renderer source.

5. **Parity catalog: render-shape only.** The catalog does not assert against any of the four lambda-deferred IPC callsites — clicking a `file://` link or loading a `file://` image src would invoke `window.maestro.*` which is absent in the test harness. Catalog stays render-shape-only per the L2.5 SessionListItem / ToggleButtonGroup precedent (the click semantics belong to feature-consumer catalogs). Five happy-path stories cover the prose-container chrome, fenced-code-block copy-button overlay, `<h1>` heading rendering, external-link anchor rendering, and unordered-list rendering. Five negative-path stories cover empty-content prose-wrapper presence, inline-code suppression of the block-code copy-button overlay, plain-paragraph non-emission of `<h1>`, `javascript:` pseudo-protocol stripping by `markdownUrlTransform`, and a lifecycle no-IPC / no-WS pin. Story floor met: 5/5 happy ≥ 3, and 5 negative ≥ 5 happy (≥1 negative-per-happy floor).

6. **Index barrel: append to existing L2.5 leaf-parade section.** Two `export` lines appended at the end of `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — one named `{ MarkdownRenderer, CodeBlockWithCopy }`, one type-only `{ CodeBlockWithCopyProps, MarkdownRendererProps }`. Barrel union-merge driver (commit `e3540a054`) handles parallel L2.5 branches mechanically.

#### Files added

- `src/webFull/components/MarkdownRenderer.tsx` (~575 LOC including the extended header documenting every import-path adjustment + the lambda-deferred renderer-surface audit).
- `src/webFull/components/MarkdownRenderer.parity.test.ts` (10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).
- This ISA append.

- `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` — one-line edit on line 68: `import { MarkdownRenderer } from '../../renderer/components/MarkdownRenderer';` → `import { MarkdownRenderer } from './MarkdownRenderer';`. This is the cross-fork-import-neutralization edit the brief explicitly requested. No other lines in the file are touched.
- `ISA.md` — this Decision entry + the new `ISC-44.layer-2.5.markdown_renderer` line as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line precedes `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages` so the lift dependency reads top-down).

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted `ThemePicker` into a webFull Settings → Display tab — the host component (`SettingsModal` Display tab) has its own transitive store / IPC dependencies (`useSettingsStore` write path, settings-broadcast wiring) and is downstream-layer scope.

- Lifting a `ThemeProvider`-backed convenience wrapper that reads the active theme + themes map from the webFull `ThemeContext` so callers don't have to thread them as props — explicitly out-of-scope per the verbatim-lift rule; that's a webFull-side composition, not a renderer parity port.
- Wiring the lifted block into the webFull tour intro overlay or first-launch empty-state host — feature wiring is a downstream-layer concern.
- Lifting the renderer's `AchievementCard` (the second consumer of `icon-wand.png` per the `grep -r icon-wand` audit) — separate component, separate brief; will re-use the same renderer-side asset import path established here.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `CollapsibleJsonViewer` lift

- **2026-06-08** — **Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `CollapsibleJsonViewer` lift.** Lifted `src/renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx` (303 LOC, 0 IPC, 0 Electron-only APIs) into `src/webFull/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx`. Branch `leaf-collapsible-json-viewer` off `main @ bf77ab942` (head of `main` after chain-merge #7 — the `leaf-context-warning-sash` merge — already in place; the just-prior `leaf-agent-error` merge `dc436bffe` is the cross-fork-import source this lift NEUTRALIZES).

#### Pre-flight

- `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx` → empty (exit 1). Confirms 0 IPC + 0 Electron-only APIs in the lifted module itself.
- Transitive dep audit: the renderer source imports `safeClipboardWrite` from `src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts`. Read confirms that function wraps `navigator.clipboard.writeText` only — pure browser API. The Electron-only surface in the same file (`window.maestro.shell.copyImageToClipboard`) is exclusively inside `safeClipboardWriteImage`, a sibling function this viewer does NOT call. The dep chain is browser-safe end-to-end. This was the same audit the prior `leaf-agent-error` lift performed before pulling the viewer across the fork by relative path; that prior conclusion stands.
- All other imports are pure (`lucide-react` icons `ChevronRight` / `ChevronDown` / `Copy` / `Check`; React `useState` / `useCallback` / `memo`).

#### Cross-fork neutralization rationale (the load-bearing reason this lift exists)

The just-merged `leaf-agent-error` wave (chain-merge #7, commit `dc436bffe`) placed `AgentErrorModal` into `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx` but left a single webFull→renderer reach in place:

```ts
import { CollapsibleJsonViewer } from '../../renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer';
```

That cross-fork import was documented at the time as an audit risk A silent-drift surface — the renderer tree is the upstream-mirror in this fork, so every webFull→renderer reach is a future rebase conflict source. The `leaf-agent-error` Decision block explicitly deferred lifting the viewer "until a second webFull consumer needs the same viewer." This brief picks that deferral up early because the first consumer's cross-fork edge is itself worth cutting — a single live consumer is sufficient justification once the viewer's transitive surface has been audited as browser-safe.

The lift moves the viewer into `src/webFull/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx`. **`AgentErrorModal` retargeting onto this webFull copy is the follow-up cleanup wave (out of scope for this brief).** Once that retargeting lands, the webFull→renderer reach for the viewer is fully cut and the audit-risk-A silent-drift surface around `AgentErrorModal`'s JSON-details panel is closed.

#### Decisions

- **Verbatim copy with two import-path adjustments, no API changes.** The renderer source is the spec; the lift preserves component name, prop shape (`data` / `theme` / `initialExpandLevel` / `maxStringLength` / `rootLabel`), default-prop values (initialExpandLevel=2, maxStringLength=100), default export, and `React.memo` wrapping at both `JsonNode` / `CopyButton` / `CollapsibleJsonViewer` boundaries. The two import-path adjustments are mechanical fork-hygiene moves only.
- **`Theme` from `src/shared/theme-types`** matching the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 sibling precedent (no `types/` aggregator in webFull yet — the renderer aggregator only re-exports the shape from `src/shared/theme-types`, so going direct is more direct and avoids the renderer-aggregator dependency entirely).
- **`safeClipboardWrite` from `../../renderer/utils/clipboard`** rather than duplicating into `src/webFull/utils/clipboard.ts`. Rationale: the audit confirms the function is a pure browser-API wrapper around `navigator.clipboard.writeText`. Duplicating a tiny browser-safe utility into webFull creates the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against — a future bug fix to one copy could miss the other. The L2.5 precedent for pulling pure renderer utility leaves by relative path is established (the `leaf-shortcuts-help` lift did this for `FIXED_SHORTCUTS`, `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS`, `getLevelForPercentage`, `fuzzyMatch`; the `leaf-agent-error` lift did this for the viewer itself; this lift continues the pattern at the next level down). The direction of the reach matters: webFull→renderer for a tiny pure utility is the L2.5-accepted pattern when the audit clears; webFull→renderer for an entire 303-LOC presentational component (the prior state) is the audit-risk-A surface this brief closes.
- **No barrel split needed; `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section.** The lift composes nothing from the L2.1 primitives (no `Modal` / `ModalFooter` / `useLayerStack`) — it is a standalone presentational tree. The `index.ts` barrel already has a "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" header opened by batch #1 and extended through chain-merge #7. This lift appends a single `export { CollapsibleJsonViewer } from './CollapsibleJsonViewer';` line under that same header. No new section header introduced. Barrel union-merge driver is live (commit `e3540a054`); the additive append composes cleanly with any parallel L2.5 branches.
- **No prop-type re-export.** The viewer's `CollapsibleJsonViewerProps` interface is intentionally not exported (the renderer source does not export it either — it is internal). Consumers thread the props inline via the component's call signature. Preserved verbatim.

#### Files added (new files only)

- `src/webFull/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.tsx` — 332 LOC including the extended header documenting the cross-fork neutralization rationale and every import-path adjustment. Component body is verbatim from the 303-LOC renderer source.
- `src/webFull/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer.parity.test.ts` — 12 stories (6 happy + 6 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor exactly at 6/6); 8 catalog-shape vitest guards. Catalog is render-shape oriented (`hasElement` + `hasText` only — click / hover / clipboard semantics belong to the future feature-consumer's catalog or to the browser-API contract, not the primitive's). Includes a "viewer is not a modal or banner" structural pin that fails the suite if any story targets `[role="dialog"]` or `[role="alert"]` directly (the `:not(:has(...))` exclusion form remains permitted as a presentational-contract guard).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { CollapsibleJsonViewer } from './CollapsibleJsonViewer';` line under the existing "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" section, immediately after the prior `ContextWarningSash` exports. Barrel union-merge driver is live (per `e3540a054` referenced in prior layer evidence), so collisions with other in-flight leaf-parade branches resolve mechanically.
- `ISA.md` — this Decision entry + the new `ISC-44.layer-2.5.collapsible_json_viewer` line under the per-feature parity-catalog section directly as `[x]` CLOSED. The prior `leaf-agent-error` "Deferred / out-of-scope" bullet that named this viewer lift is annotated as picked up here.

#### Files NOT touched (forbidden by brief / standing scope rule)

- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle for this leaf lift. **`AgentErrorModal`'s cross-fork import of the viewer remains intact in this branch by design** — retargeting it onto the webFull copy is the follow-up cleanup wave per the brief.
- `src/web/` — fork-hygiene rule; upstream-mirror web tree untouched.
- `src/main/` — no new routes; this is a purely visual leaf lift.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `GroupChatHeader` lift)

Branch `leaf-groupchat-header` cut off `main @ c0d2904f0` (post-merge of the `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift). This branch continues the GroupChat module port — `GroupChatHeader` is the direct sibling of the `GroupChatMessages` view that just landed. Lifts `src/renderer/components/GroupChatHeader.tsx` (143 LOC) verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog. The `shortcutFormatter` shim landed by the `leaf-autorunner-help` lift is the precursor infrastructure that unblocks this lift's only divergent import; this is the third consumer of that shim after `AutoRunnerHelpModal` and `GroupChatMessages`.

#### Decisions

1. **`GroupChatHeader.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/GroupChatHeader.tsx`, 143 LOC) is the chrome row above the Group Chat scrollback: chat headline + click-to-rename + pencil-icon rename button, a Stop All button (only when `state !== 'idle'`), a participant-count pill (with pluralization), an optional total-cost pill (with the incomplete-data asterisk + tooltip swap), an Info button, and an optional right-panel toggle button. Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/GroupChatHeader.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body itself touches none of the banned surface — all side effects are delivered via prop callbacks that the host wires. Lifted body-verbatim with import-path adapts only.

2. **Four import-path adapts; one webFull shim, two shared-types swaps, one renderer-types reach.** Following the L2.5 sibling precedent set by `GroupChatMessages` (the immediately prior lift):

   - `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap).
   - `GroupChatState` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/group-chat-types'` (canonical source — the renderer barrel re-exports from there; same swap `GroupChatMessages` made).
   - `Shortcut` from `'../types'` → `'../../renderer/types'` (the interface lives in the renderer types barrel only — `src/renderer/types/index.ts` line 165 — and is not yet replicated to `src/shared/`; matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` precedent of pulling specific types from the canonical aggregator rather than copying into `src/shared/` which would create the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against; `Shortcut` is a pure `{ id, label, keys }` data shape with no transitive `window.maestro` references).
   - `formatShortcutKeys` from `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` → resolves to the webFull-side shim at `'../utils/shortcutFormatter'` (path unchanged; the lifted file resolves into `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts`, which is the divergent shim, not the renderer's).

3. **No transitive `window.maestro` exposure.** The source has zero direct `window.maestro` / Electron references AND none of its imports drag any in transitively. `lucide-react` (`Info`, `Edit2`, `Columns`, `DollarSign`, `StopCircle`) is a pure icon dep already used across the webFull tree. `Theme` and `GroupChatState` are pure data shapes. `Shortcut` is a pure data shape. The single behavioural import (`formatShortcutKeys`) routes through the webFull shim. The lifted module mounts cleanly in a browser host.

4. **The `shortcutFormatter` webFull shim is the same divergence point the L2.5 GroupChatMessages lift used.** The renderer formatter's `isMacOSPlatform()` import resolves to `src/renderer/utils/platformUtils.ts`, which reads `window.maestro.platform` at module-load time. The webFull shim at `src/webFull/utils/shortcutFormatter.ts` (landed by the `leaf-autorunner-help` lift @ `a82d4012e`) swaps that one import for the `navigator.userAgent`-based webFull `isMacOSPlatform()` while keeping the formatter logic verbatim. This lift is the third consumer of that precursor infrastructure (`AutoRunnerHelpModal` first, `GroupChatMessages` second, `GroupChatHeader` now).

5. **No new barrel-section split needed; the `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section** (right under the `GroupChatMessages` lines that just landed). Exports the component only — there is no ref-handle to expose (no `forwardRef` in the source), so a single `export { GroupChatHeader }` line is sufficient.

6. **Parity catalog scope.** Ten stories (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's ">=3 happy + >=1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: headline + rename pencil + Info button baseline render with `role="button"` + `tabindex="0"` headline (`Group Chat: {name}` copy); participant pill plural form at `participantCount === 3`; Stop All button surfacing under `state === 'moderator-thinking'` with the canonical tooltip + "Stop All" copy; cost pill two-decimal rendering at `totalCost = 1.2345` with the canonical "Total accumulated cost" tooltip; right-panel toggle button surfacing under `rightPanelOpen === false` with the formatted-shortcut hint in the tooltip. Negative paths pin: Stop All suppressed under `state === 'idle'` (the `{state !== 'idle' && ...}` guard); participant pill singular form at `participantCount === 1` (the `!== 1 ? 's' : ''` ternary); cost pill fully suppressed when `totalCost === 0` (the `totalCost > 0` guard — both the standard tooltip variant and the incomplete-data variant are absent); incomplete-cost asterisk + tooltip variant surfacing under `costIncomplete === true` (the `costIncomplete && '*'` token and the swapped `title` copy); right-panel toggle suppressed under `rightPanelOpen === true` (the `{!rightPanelOpen && ...}` guard). Six catalog-shape vitest guards: >=3 stories, >=3 happy stories, >=1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `dialog.` / `tunnel.` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body).

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- **Retargeting `src/webFull/components/AgentErrorModal.tsx`'s `CollapsibleJsonViewer` import** from `'../../renderer/components/CollapsibleJsonViewer'` → `'./CollapsibleJsonViewer'`. This is the follow-up cleanup wave that fully closes the audit-risk-A surface. Out of scope for this brief by explicit instruction ("After this lands, AgentErrorModal can be retargeted to use the webFull copy in a follow-up.").
- **Duplicating `safeClipboardWrite` into `src/webFull/utils/`** — rejected per the precedent above; the cross-fork pull of a tiny browser-safe utility is the L2.5-accepted pattern. If a future audit pass duplicates the utility into webFull, that is its own lift wave with its own ISC.
- **Feature wiring into a webFull consumer** — the viewer ships as latent surface area for L2.6+ feature consumers (the AgentErrorModal retargeting is the first; other future webFull surfaces displaying structured payloads — e.g. observability event details, MCP tool response viewer — could compose this same primitive).
- **Lift surface 0-IPC + 0-Electron-API confirmation (module-load time):**
  - `grep -E "from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/webFull/components/MarkdownRenderer.tsx` → empty.
  - The four `window.maestro.*` callsites are present verbatim (line 117 + 360 + 362 + 373) and live inside `useEffect` / `onClick` lambda bodies per the audit above. Brief's lambda-deferred acceptance rule applies.

Catalog declares 10 stories total (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" minimum), uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary, and passes the IPC-leakage guard.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

Deferred until a webFull-side consumer actually exercises those codepaths and needs them to work.
- Neutralizing the remaining five cross-fork imports inside `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` (`textProcessing`, `participantColors`, `markdownConfig` for `generateTerminalProseStyles`, `clipboard`, `formatShortcutKeys`-shaped utility callsites) — each is its own pre-flight pass and own brief; doing all six in one branch would balloon scope beyond leaf-parade.
- Lifting the renderer's `LocalImage` cache to a webFull-side IndexedDB-backed store — the renderer source uses a module-scope `Map<string, string>` which works fine for the current usage pattern; an upgrade is downstream-layer scope.
- Lifting `safeClipboardWrite` / `safeClipboardWriteImage` (`src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts`) to a webFull-side shim that swaps the `window.maestro.shell.copyImageToClipboard` fallback for browser-native `navigator.clipboard.write(...)` — listed as deferred in the GroupChatMessages lift; this branch doesn't change that posture.

  - `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ | wc -c` → 0 (read-only oracles + main process untouched).
