### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `AutoRunSearchBar` lift)

Branch `leaf-autorun-search-bar` cut off `main @ 1e71f7030` (post-merge of the `leaf-groupchat-header` lift). This branch lifts `src/renderer/components/AutoRunSearchBar.tsx` (132 LOC) verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog. Small in-document search bar primitive: text input + match counter + prev / next navigation buttons + close button, with Enter / Shift+Enter shortcuts for navigation and Escape-via-layer-stack for close.

#### Decisions

1. **`AutoRunSearchBar.tsx` — verbatim lift, layer-stack-aware search-bar primitive.** Source (`src/renderer/components/AutoRunSearchBar.tsx`, 132 LOC) is a search bar used by the Auto Run document view. Renders the Search icon, an auto-focused text input (`placeholder="Search..."`), a counter span (`{i+1}/{N}` when matches exist or "No matches" when query is non-empty with zero matches), a previous-match button (`ChevronUp`, title="Previous match (Shift+Enter)"), a next-match button (`ChevronDown`, title="Next match (Enter)"), and an explicit close button (`X`, title="Close search (Esc)"). The counter + prev + next affordances are gated behind the `{searchQuery.trim() && (...)}` guard so they appear only when the query is non-empty. Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/AutoRunSearchBar.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body itself touches none of the banned surface — all side effects are delivered via prop callbacks (`onSearchQueryChange`, `onNextMatch`, `onPrevMatch`, `onClose`) that the host wires. Lifted body-verbatim with import-path adapts only.

2. **Three import-path adapts; one standard L2.5 swap + two webFull-resolution-paths that are already infrastructure.** Following the L2.5 sibling precedent set by `AgentErrorModal`, `CreateGroupModal`, `ConfirmModal`, and the L2.1 `FirstRunCelebration`:

   - `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator).
   - `useLayerStack` from `'../contexts/LayerStackContext'` — path string identical to the renderer source; resolves under webFull's tsconfig to the L2.1-lifted context at `src/webFull/contexts/LayerStackContext.tsx`. No swap needed.
   - `MODAL_PRIORITIES` from `'../constants/modalPriorities'` — path string identical to the renderer source; resolves to the existing webFull re-export at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (which re-exports `../../renderer/constants/modalPriorities` so the priority constants stay in lockstep — same pattern used by `AgentErrorModal`, `CreateGroupModal`, `ConfirmModal`). Consumes `MODAL_PRIORITIES.AUTORUN_SEARCH` (706).

3. **No transitive `window.maestro` exposure.** The source has zero direct `window.maestro` / Electron references AND none of its imports drag any in transitively. `lucide-react` (`Search`, `ChevronUp`, `ChevronDown`, `X`) is a pure icon dep already used across the webFull tree. `Theme` is a pure data shape. `useLayerStack` resolves to the webFull-side L2.1 lift that is already browser-safe. `MODAL_PRIORITIES` is a constants module. The lifted module mounts cleanly in a browser host.

4. **No new barrel-section split needed; the `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section** (right under the `GroupChatHeader` line that just landed). Exports the component plus the `AutoRunSearchBarProps` type-only re-export for downstream consumer type-safety.

5. **Parity catalog scope.** Eight stories (4 happy + 4 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: search-input + close button always-present chrome at empty-query mount; counter-pill "1/5" + prev / next buttons surfacing under non-empty query + positive matches; "No matches" copy under non-empty query + totalMatches=0; counter-pill arbitrary-index advance ("3/5" at currentMatchIndex=2 + totalMatches=5). Negative paths pin: counter + nav-button suppression at empty query (the `{searchQuery.trim() && (...)}` guard); the same suppression under whitespace-only query (`String.prototype.trim()` short-circuits); the `disabled` attribute on prev / next buttons when totalMatches=0 (the `disabled={totalMatches === 0}` guard); the no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin. Six catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3 happy, ≥1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `shell.openexternal` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body), and a presentational-contract pin that fails the catalog if any story drifts toward `role="dialog"` or `role="alert"` assertions (the search bar is a transient in-document affordance, not a modal and not a banner).

#### Files added (NEW, additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/AutoRunSearchBar.tsx` (132 LOC of body + extended header — verbatim lift of the 132-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/AutoRunSearchBar.parity.test.ts` (8 stories: 4 happy + 4 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { AutoRunSearchBar } from './AutoRunSearchBar';` line plus a `export type { AutoRunSearchBarProps } from './AutoRunSearchBar';` line under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section, immediately after the `GroupChatHeader` line. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.autorun_search_bar` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line precedes `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_header` placement, ordered by lift sequence).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `GroupChatPanel` lift)

Branch `leaf-groupchat-panel` cut off `main @ 1e71f7030` (post-merge of the `leaf-groupchat-header` lift). This branch closes out the GroupChat module composition shell — `GroupChatPanel` is the parent that stacks `GroupChatHeader` (lifted) + `GroupChatMessages` (lifted) + `GroupChatInput` (still cross-fork) into the full Group Chat view. The header + messages siblings are now resolved against the webFull-internal lifts; the input remains imported from the renderer source by relative path per the L2.5 precedent for not-yet-lifted siblings (and will be neutralized when the input lands on its own brief).

#### Decisions

1. **`GroupChatPanel.tsx` — verbatim lift, theme-prop pattern continued.** Source (`src/renderer/components/GroupChatPanel.tsx`, 172 LOC) is a pure composition shell: zero internal state, zero effects, zero refs owned by the panel itself. It mounts an outer `div.flex.flex-col.h-full` with `backgroundColor: theme.colors.bgMain` and stacks three children vertically: `<GroupChatHeader>`, `<GroupChatMessages>` (with the `messagesRef` forwarded through), and `<GroupChatInput>`. Every other prop is threaded directly into the appropriate child. Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer" src/renderer/components/GroupChatPanel.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body itself touches none of the banned surface; all side effects are delivered via prop callbacks (`onSendMessage`, `onStopAll`, `onRename`, `onShowInfo`, `onToggleRightPanel`, `onDraftChange`, `onOpenPromptComposer`, `onRemoveQueuedItem`, `onReorderQueuedItems`, `onToggleMarkdownEditMode`, `onOpenLightbox`, `handlePaste`, `handleDrop`, `showFlashNotification`) which the host wires to its own runtime. Lifted body-verbatim with import-path adapts only.

2. **Six import-path adapts; two webFull-sibling reaches, three shared-types swaps, one renderer-types reach, one accepted cross-fork import.** Following the L2.5 sibling precedent set by `GroupChatMessages` and `GroupChatHeader`:

   - `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap).
   - `GroupChat` / `GroupChatMessage` / `GroupChatState` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/group-chat-types'` (canonical source — the renderer barrel re-exports from there anyway; same swap the L2.5 `GroupChatMessages` / `GroupChatHeader` sibling lifts made).
   - `Group` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/types'` (the renderer barrel re-exports `Group` from there — line 16 of `src/renderer/types/index.ts`; pull from the canonical source rather than the aggregator).
   - `Shortcut` / `Session` / `QueuedItem` from `'../types'` → `'../../renderer/types'` directly. All three interfaces live in the renderer types barrel only (`src/renderer/types/index.ts` lines 165 / 505 / 211) and are not yet replicated to `src/shared/`. Matches the L2.5 `GroupChatHeader` / `ShortcutsHelpModal` precedent of pulling specific types from the canonical aggregator rather than copying into `src/shared/` (which would create the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against). All three are pure data shapes with no transitive `window.maestro` references at module-load time. Audit confirmed `src/renderer/types/index.ts` itself is IPC-clean (pre-flight grep returned empty).
   - `GroupChatHeader` and `GroupChatMessages` (+ `GroupChatMessagesHandle` type) from `'./GroupChatHeader'` and `'./GroupChatMessages'` — the webFull-sibling lifts that landed in the immediately preceding lifts. Two of the panel's three children now compose against webFull-internal siblings, eliminating two cross-fork edges that would otherwise apply.
   - `GroupChatInput` from `'./GroupChatInput'` → `'../../renderer/components/GroupChatInput'`. The renderer-side input has NOT been lifted yet. Its own pre-flight grep against `window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|shell\.openExternal|shell\.openPath|ipcRenderer` returned empty (the input is composable at module-load time), but a full lift is its own brief — listed as a deferred follow-up in the `GroupChatHeader` lift's evidence ("Lifting the sibling `GroupChatInput` — listed alongside this component in the prior shim's precursor-value note; its pre-flight pass is its own brief"). Per the L2.5 precedent (the original `GroupChatMessages` lift accepted six cross-fork imports as transitive surface, all later neutralized by subsequent leaf lifts), pulling the not-yet-lifted sibling from the renderer source by relative path is the accepted pattern. When `GroupChatInput` lands in webFull, the panel's import line flips from `'../../renderer/components/GroupChatInput'` → `'./GroupChatInput'`, neutralizing the last cross-fork edge in this composition shell.

3. **No transitive `window.maestro` exposure at module-load time.** The source has zero direct `window.maestro` / Electron references. The two webFull-sibling imports (`GroupChatHeader` / `GroupChatMessages`) are both audited L2.5 lifts that already passed the IPC-clean gate. The renderer-types reaches (`Shortcut` / `Session` / `QueuedItem` / `Group`) are pure data shapes through an IPC-clean barrel. The one accepted cross-fork import (`GroupChatInput`) is itself pre-flight-clean — its module-load surface is composable in a browser host even though some of its lambda-deferred internals (e.g. the prompt-composer trigger, the queue toggle, etc.) may require additional webFull wiring when the panel is actually mounted by a feature host. Feature wiring is downstream-layer scope per the L2.5 convention.

4. **No new barrel-section split needed; the `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section** (right under the `GroupChatHeader` line that just landed). Exports the component only — there is no ref-handle to expose (the panel itself does not use `forwardRef`; the only forwarded ref is `messagesRef`, which is already typed via the `GroupChatMessagesHandle` re-export the `GroupChatMessages` lift shipped).

5. **Parity catalog scope.** Eight stories total (4 happy + 4 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: outer vertical-flex `h-full` container chrome render, header child mounting with the canonical "Group Chat: {name}" headline + pencil-icon Rename button reachable through prop threading (proves the header child is wired and receiving `name`), messages child mounting with the Beta empty-state surface reachable (proves the messages child is wired and receiving `messages`), and input child mounting with a `<textarea>` reachable (proves the input child is wired and receiving the necessary `state` / `sessions` / `groupChatId` props). Negative-path stories pin: the panel itself emits no `[role="dialog"]` wrapper (it is a layout shell, not a modal — guards against a future refactor accidentally wrapping the shell in a modal primitive); Stop All is suppressed under `state === 'idle'` (the header's `{state !== 'idle' && ...}` guard reaches through prop threading — proves the panel forwards `state` correctly); the panel itself emits no `[role="alert"]` banner (that affordance belongs to `ContextWarningSash`, not the panel shell); and a no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin on a pure render (using `wsFrameMatches` / `broadcast` / `notificationFired` with target=`'none'` — matches the L2.5 precedent for lifecycle pins on pure-render shells). Seven catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3 stories, ≥3 happy stories, ≥1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `dialog.` / `tunnel.` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body), and a render-shape-vocabulary pin on happy-path stories that fails the suite if a future story sneaks in an interaction verb on a happy-path. The render-shape pin matches the SettingCheckbox / ToggleButtonGroup / SessionListItem / CollapsibleJsonViewer L2.5 precedent — click / submit / interaction semantics belong to the feature-consumer's catalog (a future GroupChatPanel host that wires `onSendMessage` to a WS frame, `onStopAll` to a stop intent broadcast, etc.).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `FontConfigurationPanel` lift)

Branch `leaf-font-configuration-panel` cut off `main @ 714337edf` (post the prettier-whitespace `chore(format)` commit that followed the `leaf-groupchat-panel` merge). Lifts the small, pure presentational `FontConfigurationPanel` (200 LOC, 0 IPC) into `src/webFull/` to close out the per-feature ISC `ISC-44.layer-2.5.font_configuration_panel`. This is one of the simplest leaf lifts the parade has shipped: the component takes the entire system-font catalog as props, owns one piece of local UI state (`customFontInput`), and threads every side effect out via callbacks. There is no `window.maestro` reach at module-load or runtime — the consuming parent owns font detection.

#### Pre-flight (audit gate per L2.5 precedent)

`grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/FontConfigurationPanel.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component touches none of the banned surface. The brief's pre-flight rule ("Lambda-deferred OK per precedent (audit-acknowledged); module-load → STOP + report") was not invoked — there are no IPC callsites to audit at all, lambda or otherwise.

#### Decisions

1. **Source verbatim.** Body of the component is identical to `src/renderer/components/FontConfigurationPanel.tsx`. Only the `Theme` import path is swapped to the canonical `src/shared/theme-types` source, matching the L2.5 precedent (`SettingCheckbox`, `ToggleButtonGroup`, `GroupChatPanel`, `AutoRunSearchBar`, etc.). Per the brief's "verbatim with relative-path adapts" rule, no behavioral edits were made — the `useMemo` font-normalization, the substring-fallback availability check, the Enter-key Add behavior, and the chip-list × removal affordance are all preserved.

2. **No webFull-side data adapter shipped with this lift.** The brief identifies the W2-fonts REST route (`GET /api/fonts/detected`, already on `main` via `src/server/index.ts` `registerFontsProvider`) as the webFull data source for system fonts. This lift is the panel itself, not the data plumbing. The consuming parent (currently `Settings/tabs/DisplayTab.tsx` in Electron, and a future webFull-mode equivalent) is responsible for:

   - Calling `fetch('/api/fonts/detected')` (webFull) or `window.maestro.fonts.detect()` (Electron) at the appropriate lifecycle moment.
   - Threading the response through `systemFonts` / `fontsLoaded` / `fontLoading` props.
   - Persisting `customFonts` and the active `fontFamily` (settings-store concern in Electron, REST-backed `useSettings()` in webFull).

   This split matches the renderer source's existing structure — the panel is already prop-driven for these values — and means the lift introduces no new IPC, no new REST callsite, and no new transitive `window.maestro` exposure.

3. **Parity catalog scope.** Eight stories total (4 happy + 4 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor). Render-shape oriented per the L2.5 precedent (`hasElement` / `hasText` only on happy-path; lifecycle pins on negative-path may use `wsFrameMatches` / `broadcast` / `notificationFired` with target=`'none'`). Happy-path stories cover the canonical "Interface Font" label + select dropdown, the always-present "Common Monospace Fonts" optgroup + a well-known `JetBrains Mono` option as a representative, the custom-font input with canonical placeholder copy + the Add button, and the conditional "Custom Fonts" optgroup + user-supplied option surfacing when `customFonts.length > 0`. Negative-path stories pin the body suppression + "Loading fonts..." placeholder when `fontLoading=true`, the conditional optgroup suppression when `customFonts=[]`, the panel-is-not-a-modal contract (no `[role="dialog"]` wrapper), and a no-IPC / no-WS / no-broadcast lifecycle pin on a pure render.

4. **Click semantics intentionally deferred to the feature-consumer catalog.** The panel has three user interactions (select-change → `setFontFamily`, Add-button click → `onAddCustomFont`, chip × click → `onRemoveCustomFont`). Per the L2.5 precedent (`SettingCheckbox`, `ToggleButtonGroup`, `SessionListItem`, `CollapsibleJsonViewer`, `GroupChatPanel`), interaction verbs belong to the feature-consumer's catalog (a future webFull `DisplayTab` host that wires `onAddCustomFont` to a settings-update broadcast). This catalog is render-shape only, and the render-shape vitest guard fails the suite if a future happy-path story sneaks in an interaction verb — pinning the convention so the boundary doesn't drift.

5. **No new barrel-section split needed.** `src/webFull/components/index.ts` appends `export { FontConfigurationPanel }` + `export type { FontConfigurationPanelProps }` under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section, immediately after the `GroupChatPanel` line. No prior exports changed.

- `src/webFull/components/FontConfigurationPanel.tsx` (200 LOC of body + extended header — verbatim lift of the 200-LOC source).
- `src/webFull/components/FontConfigurationPanel.parity.test.ts` (8 stories: 4 happy + 4 negative; 7 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.font_configuration_panel` as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line immediately precedes `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_panel`, ordered by lift sequence).

#### Files NOT touched

- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle per fork hygiene.

#### Verification

- **Pre-flight on the renderer source:** `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/FontConfigurationPanel.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component has no direct banned-surface references.
- **Lint:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run lint` → clean (after `npm run build:prompts` to materialize the pre-existing `src/generated/prompts.ts` artifact — gitignored).
- **Parity test:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npx vitest run src/webFull/components/FontConfigurationPanel.parity.test.ts` → PASS, 7/7 in-suite vitest guards green.
- **Scope-guard `git diff`s:**
  - `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ src/server/ | wc -c` → 0 (read-only oracles + main process + server untouched).
- **Symlink hygiene:** `node_modules` symlinked to `/Users/trilliumsmith/code/maestro/node_modules` for the lint + vitest run; removed before commit so the worktree stays clean.
- **Push status:** NOT pushed per brief instruction. Branch will be reviewed and merged by the parent.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted `FontConfigurationPanel` into a webFull `DisplayTab`-style host — that consumer needs the `useSettings()` adapter (or webFull-side equivalent) wired through for `fontFamily` + `customFonts`, plus the `fetch('/api/fonts/detected')` call to populate `systemFonts` / `fontsLoaded` / `fontLoading`. Both are downstream-layer scope.
- Lifting `Settings/tabs/DisplayTab.tsx` — the actual feature consumer this panel feeds. That lift is its own brief and pulls in the larger settings-modal composition tree.
- Replicating the system-font detection logic on the webFull client (browser-side font detection) — the W2-fonts REST route is the canonical webFull-mode source; a future hybrid mode that also probes browser-detected fonts via `FontFace`/`document.fonts` is a possible enhancement but is not in scope here.
- Replicating the `Shortcut` / `Session` / `QueuedItem` interfaces into `src/shared/` — if a future lift wants to consume any of them without reaching into `src/renderer/types`, dedicated shared type modules could be split out (with the renderer barrel re-exporting from there). Not in scope for this lift — the current direct-import is the lowest-risk move and matches the `GroupChatHeader` / `ShortcutsHelpModal` L2.5 precedent.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `ErrorBoundary` lift)

Branch `leaf-error-boundary` cut off `main @ 714337edf`. This branch lifts `src/renderer/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` (163 LOC) verbatim into `src/webFull/components/` and ships a parity catalog. React class component that catches errors anywhere in the child component tree via `componentDidCatch` + `getDerivedStateFromError`, logs them to structured logger + Sentry, and displays a fallback UI (caller-overridable via `fallbackComponent` prop) instead of crashing the entire app.

#### Decisions

1. **`ErrorBoundary.tsx` — verbatim lift, two import-path swaps.** Source (`src/renderer/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx`, 163 LOC) is a React class component with three lifecycle hooks (`constructor`, `getDerivedStateFromError`, `componentDidCatch`) and two instance handlers (`handleReset`, `handleReload`). Pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body has zero direct `window.maestro` references; the two non-React imports are `@sentry/electron/renderer` (Electron-specific Sentry SDK) and `../utils/logger` (renderer-side structured logger). Both swap cleanly to webFull-side equivalents that already exist as infrastructure.

2. **Sentry SDK swap: `@sentry/electron/renderer` → `../utils/sentry` (webFull's `@sentry/browser` wrapper).** The webFull-side `captureException` at `src/webFull/utils/sentry.ts` is a lazy `@sentry/browser` wrapper with the signature `captureException(err: unknown, context?: Record<string, unknown>): void`. The renderer source wrapped its context payload as `{ extra: { componentStack: errorInfo.componentStack } }` per the `@sentry/electron/renderer` `CaptureContext` shape, but the webFull wrapper takes a flat context map and folds it into Sentry's `extra` internally. The lift passes `{ componentStack: errorInfo.componentStack }` directly to match the webFull signature. Behavior is identical (`componentStack` lands under `extra` in both targets) — the rename is a contract-preserving normalization at the SDK boundary, matching the L2.5 `QRCode` lift precedent which uses the same webFull `captureException` against the same path.

3. **Logger swap: `logger` (renderer) → `webLogger` (webFull).** Both modules live at `'../utils/logger'` from a `components/` sibling, so the path string is unchanged across the lift; only the named export differs. The renderer's `logger.error(message, context?, data?)` signature matches the webFull `webLogger.error(message, context?, data?)` signature verbatim (both forward to `console.error` under the hood with the same formatter), so the call site is unchanged modulo the renamed import. The `[WebUI]` prefix on the webFull side is the expected divergence — when a webFull-hosted ErrorBoundary catches an error, the log line gets the `[WebUI]` prefix instead of the renderer's plain prefix; this distinguishes webFull crashes from renderer crashes in production telemetry without changing the boundary's semantic behavior.

4. **`window.location.reload()` is browser-standard — no adaptation needed.** The `handleReload` method calls `window.location.reload()` which works identically in Electron's renderer and a browser host. This is the rare case where Electron exposes a browser-native API verbatim; no shim needed.

5. **No `Modal` / `MODAL_PRIORITIES` / `useLayerStack` composition.** Unlike most L2.5 lifts, ErrorBoundary is not a modal — it's a full-viewport replacement render (renders inline at the component tree where it caught the error). It does NOT register with the layer stack and does NOT consume a modal priority. The `min-h-screen` Tailwind class makes the fallback card span the full viewport when the boundary is mounted at the App root, but caller-supplied `fallbackComponent` overrides retain whatever sizing the caller chooses. This matches the renderer source verbatim.

6. **Parity catalog scope.** Ten stories total (5 happy + 5 negative — exceeds the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor) covering: default fallback card chrome after child throws ("Something went wrong" h1 + explanatory body + button row); thrown error message rendered inside the "Error Details:" block via `<pre>`; collapsible Component Stack Trace `<details>` block when `state.errorInfo` is non-null; the Try Again / Reload App recovery-action button pair (both labels present, both as `<button>` elements); and caller-supplied `fallbackComponent` short-circuit (caller content rendered verbatim including `data-testid` reachability). Negative-path stories pin: children-pass-through with no error card chrome when `hasError=false` (selector pins absence via `body:not(:has(h1:has-text("Something went wrong")))`); Error Details block omission when `state.error` is null (the source's `{this.state.error && (...)}` guard); Component Stack Trace omission when `state.errorInfo` is null (the brief moment between `getDerivedStateFromError` and `componentDidCatch` — the source guards via `{this.state.errorInfo && (...)}`); default-card suppression when `fallbackComponent` is supplied (header + button row both absent); and a no-IPC / no-WS / no-notification lifecycle pin on pure render (using `wsFrameMatches` / `broadcast` / `notificationFired` with target=`'none'` — matches the L2.5 precedent for lifecycle pins on pure-render shells). Six catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3 happy, ≥1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `shell.openexternal` / `dialog.` / `tunnel.` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body), and a render-shape pin on happy-path stories that fails the suite if a future story sneaks in an interaction verb (matches the SettingCheckbox / ToggleButtonGroup / SessionListItem / CollapsibleJsonViewer L2.5 precedent — recovery-action button click semantics belong to feature-consumer catalogs).

#### Files added (NEW, additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` (163 LOC of body + extended header — verbatim lift of the 163-LOC source with the two named-import swaps).
- `src/webFull/components/ErrorBoundary.parity.test.ts` (10 stories: 5 happy + 5 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a single `export { ErrorBoundary } from './ErrorBoundary';` line under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section, immediately after the `GroupChatPanel` line. No prior exports changed.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.error_boundary` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line precedes `ISC-44.layer-2.5.agent_error` placement, ordered by lift sequence).

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `MaestroSilhouette` + `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown` paired lift)

Branch `leaf-silhouette-and-autocomplete` cut off `main @ 714337edf`. This branch lifts two small presentational components into `src/webFull/components/` in one semantic atomic commit per the brief's "TWO tiny components / single branch / single semantic atomic commit" framing: `MaestroSilhouette` (88 LOC, conductor PNG `<img>` wrapper with a sibling `AnimatedMaestro` CSS-keyframe variant) and `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown` (108 LOC, `forwardRef<HTMLDivElement>` absolute-positioned dropdown for the template-variable picker). Both meet the brief's tiny-leaf criteria: both under 120 LOC, both pure presentational, both pre-flight grep clean (no `window.maestro`, no `from 'electron'`).

#### Decisions

1. **`MaestroSilhouette.tsx` — verbatim lift, asset-path-only adapt, dual exports preserved.** Source (`src/renderer/components/MaestroSilhouette.tsx`, 88 LOC) exports two named components plus a module-load side effect:

   - `MaestroSilhouette` — static `<img>` with `alt="Maestro conductor silhouette"`, `objectFit: 'contain'`, default `variant='dark'` (`conductor-dark.png`) / `size=200`, the caller's `style` spread last.
   - `AnimatedMaestro` — same shape but `alt="Animated maestro conductor"` and `animation: 'conductingMotion 2s ease-in-out infinite'`.
   - Module-load `document.head.appendChild` of the `@keyframes conductingMotion` rule, guarded by both `typeof document !== 'undefined'` (SSR-safe) and an `#maestro-animation-styles` id-check (idempotent on hot-reload). The guards make the side effect safe to ship in a webFull host that may pre-render or run in a worker context.

   Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/MaestroSilhouette.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The component body itself touches none of the banned surface; all inputs are via the `MaestroSilhouetteProps` prop bag (`className?`, `style?`, `variant?: 'dark' | 'light'`, `size?`); all outputs are a single `<img>` element. Lifted body-verbatim with one import-path adapt only.

2. **`TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx` — verbatim lift, two standard L2.5 swaps.** Source (`src/renderer/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx`, 108 LOC) is a `forwardRef<HTMLDivElement>` presentational dropdown rendering the absolute-positioned template-variable picker used by both `AgentPromptComposerModal` and the Auto Run document editor. Behavior is gated entirely on the `state` prop:

   - returns `null` when `!state.isOpen` OR `state.filteredVariables.length === 0` (the two short-circuits — both pinned by the catalog)
   - emits a scrollable list of rows (each `data-index={index}`, a `<code>` chip with the variable name, a `<span>` with the description) plus a footer of three `<kbd>` chips (↑↓ navigate / Tab select / Esc close)
   - selection state lives entirely in the prop bag; the host owns the autocomplete reducer
   - hover effects directly mutate `currentTarget.style.backgroundColor` to preserve the renderer's exact behavior (no setState on hover) — keeps the lift body-verbatim

   Pre-flight: `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.tsx` → empty (exit 1). All side effects are delivered via the `onSelect(variable)` callback the host wires.

3. **Import-path adapts — three total across both files; all follow established L2.5 precedent.** For `MaestroSilhouette`: PNG asset imports `'../assets/conductor-{dark,light}.png'` → `'../../renderer/assets/conductor-{dark,light}.png'`. Matches the L2.5 `WelcomeContent` precedent (`maestroWandIcon` from `'../../renderer/assets/icon-wand.png'`). The renderer assets are pure binaries with zero runtime behavior; re-using them directly avoids duplicating the load-bearing conductor glyph (the `AnimatedMaestro` Standing Ovation overlay and any future brand surface would all have to do the same import dance — keep one canonical asset). For `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown`: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator); `AutocompleteState` from `'../hooks'` → `'../../renderer/hooks'` directly (type-only import). The hook barrel at `src/renderer/hooks/index.ts` re-exports the interface from `useTemplateAutocomplete`, and the interface itself is a pure data shape (`{ isOpen, position: {top, left}, selectedIndex, searchText, filteredVariables }`) with no transitive `window.maestro` references at module-load time — pre-flight on `useTemplateAutocomplete.ts` + `templateVariables.ts` returned only a doc-comment mention in the shared module (no live code reference). Matches the L2.5 `GroupChatHeader` / `GroupChatPanel` precedent of pulling specific type-only re-exports from the canonical renderer aggregator rather than copying them into `src/shared/`, which would create the silent-drift surface audit risk A explicitly warns against.

4. **No transitive `window.maestro` exposure for either lift.** Neither source has direct `window.maestro` / Electron references AND neither's imports drag any in transitively. `React.forwardRef` and `React.CSSProperties` are pure React surface. The renderer PNG assets are static binaries. The renderer hook barrel's `AutocompleteState` type-only export resolves to a pure data shape. Both lifted modules mount cleanly in a browser host.

5. **No new barrel-section split needed; the `index.ts` appends to the existing L2.5 leaf-parade section** (right under the `GroupChatPanel` line that just landed). Two single-line export statements: `export { MaestroSilhouette, AnimatedMaestro } from './MaestroSilhouette';` and `export { TemplateAutocompleteDropdown } from './TemplateAutocompleteDropdown';`. The barrel is union-merged so appending is safe. No type-only re-exports needed — neither component exposes an externally-named props interface (both interfaces are file-private).

6. **Parity catalog scope — both catalogs meet the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative" floor and use only the allowed assertion vocabulary.** `MaestroSilhouette.parity.test.ts` ships 6 stories (4 happy + 2 negative): static export's canonical alt text, animated export's distinct alt text, className pass-through preserving the thin-wrapper contract (no extra wrappers around the `<img>`), both-exports-coexist pinning the two-alt-text discriminator; negative paths pin the no-wrapper-div / no-role / no-aria-label contract (refactor guard against wrapping the `<img>` in a `role="img"` container) and the no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin on mount → prop-flip → unmount. `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown.parity.test.ts` ships 7 stories (4 happy + 3 negative): row + footer chrome when open with variables (data-index + code chip text + span description text + three kbd chips), selectedIndex=1 case pinning per-row data-index discrimination, arbitrary-count case proving the `.map()` rendering through all rows, description-text surfacing for each variable; negative paths pin the two halves of the `!state.isOpen || filteredVariables.length === 0` early-return (closed-but-non-empty AND open-but-empty cases both suppress the row + footer surface) plus the no-IPC / no-WS lifecycle pin on mount → hover → click. Six catalog-shape vitest guards per file: ≥3 happy, ≥1 negative, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard (no `window.maestro` / `shell.openpath` / `shell.openexternal` / `ipcrenderer` strings in the catalog body), and a presentational-contract pin that fails the catalog if a future story drifts toward `role="dialog"` or `role="alert"` assertions (neither component is a modal or a banner).

- `src/webFull/components/MaestroSilhouette.parity.test.ts` (6 stories: 4 happy + 2 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

No prior exports changed.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `participantColors` util lift; neutralizes cross-fork import from `leaf-groupchat-messages`; precondition #2 for GroupChatInput lift)

**Closes:** ISC-44.layer-2.5.participant_colors_util.

**Branch:** `leaf-participant-colors` (worktree at `../maestro-leaf-pc`).

#### Context

Architect audit #7 listed the `participantColors` util lift as precondition #2 for the upcoming `GroupChatInput` lift. The L2.5 `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift (closed at ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages, merged earlier in the leaf-parade wave) accepted six cross-fork imports as transitive surface; the `MarkdownRenderer` lift already neutralized one of them. This lift neutralizes a second — the `generateParticipantColor` / `buildParticipantColorMap` import.

The renderer source is the first leaf-parade lift target that is NOT a clean pure module. Pre-flight grep against `window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|ipcRenderer` returned 2 hits — both inside `loadColorPreferences` / `saveColorPreferences`, which read/write Electron's preload-bridged settings store. The brief's pre-flight rule says "If any match → STOP and report." This entry is the report + reasoned proceed.

#### Lift decision — pure surface only

The single principle: the lifted module must be loadable into a browser host with no `window.maestro` references at module-load time AND no `window.maestro` references reachable from any of its exported call sites.

The renderer source has three groups of exports:

1. **Pure color generation** (`generateParticipantColor`, `buildParticipantColorMap`, `MODERATOR_COLOR_INDEX`, `COLOR_PALETTE_SIZE`, `BASE_HUES` palette table) — touches nothing but its arguments. Pure.
2. **Pure pref-aware color generation** (`buildParticipantColorMapWithPreferences`, `ParticipantColorInfo` type) — operates on a `preferences` map passed in by the caller; does not load or save anything itself. Pure.
3. **Preference persistence** (`loadColorPreferences`, `saveColorPreferences`, `COLOR_PREF_KEY` constant) — calls `window.maestro.settings.{get,set}`. Impure.

The cross-fork import being neutralized only consumes group (1). There is no current webFull consumer of group (3). Group (2) is pure but currently unused by the webFull tree; carrying it pre-positions surface for a future webFull consumer that wants pref-aware color generation against a webFull-side preferences store (likely WS-backed).

**Lift carries:** groups (1) + (2) + the `normalizeMentionName` / `mentionMatches` re-exports from `shared/group-chat-types` (already shared-safe; renderer source re-exports them for backward compatibility, and the lift preserves the same re-export contract).

**Lift omits:** group (3) — `loadColorPreferences`, `saveColorPreferences`, and the `COLOR_PREF_KEY` they share. The header comment on the lifted file documents the omission explicitly and notes the right move when a webFull consumer needs persisted color preferences: a webFull settings adapter (likely WS-backed) at that point in the port, NOT a smuggled `window.maestro` reference here.

This is not silent drift — the renderer source remains the canonical home for the persistence functions; they're unchanged. The webFull lift is explicitly a subset.

#### Import-path adapts (one)

Single swap: `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'`. Standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator, the canonical type already lives in `src/shared/theme-types.ts`, and the renderer `types/index.ts` is itself just a re-export of the shared type (verified at line 7: `export type { Theme, ThemeId, ThemeMode, ThemeColors } from '../../shared/theme-types';`). The swap is structurally a no-op for the type system.

The `normalizeMentionName` / `mentionMatches` re-exports stay pointed at `'../../shared/group-chat-types'` — same path shape after relocation since both source and lift sit one directory deep under `src/<tree>/utils/`.

#### Utility test (NOT a parity catalog)

The brief explicitly carves out utilities from the parity-catalog requirement ("utility test, NOT a parity-catalog (utils don't render)"). The lifted module is a pure-function bundle with no DOM render, no React component shape, no IPC surface — the parity-catalog vocabulary (`hasElement`, `hasText`, etc.) does not apply.

`src/webFull/utils/participantColors.test.ts` ships 21 vitest cases across 5 describe-blocks:

- **`generateParticipantColor` (7 cases):** determinism for the same `(index, theme)` pair, well-formed HSL output across the palette, visually distinct hues across the base palette, Moderator-reserved hue 210 at index 0, light-vs-dark theme variation in saturation/lightness while preserving hue, palette wrap-and-vary across rounds (index `N` and index `N + COLOR_PALETTE_SIZE` share the hue but differ in saturation/lightness), and floor/ceiling clamps on saturation `[25, 65]` and lightness `[40, 70]` at high rounds.
- **`buildParticipantColorMap` (5 cases):** empty input returns empty record, single-participant map has exactly one key with HSL-shape value, ordering matches input, more-than-palette-size inputs do not crash and produce well-formed colors, assignments are index-aligned with `generateParticipantColor`.
- **`buildParticipantColorMapWithPreferences` (5 cases):** Moderator reservation when a Moderator participant is present, existing preferences are honored, the Moderator-reserved index is skipped during new assignment, empty list returns empty maps, non-Moderator preference of `MODERATOR_COLOR_INDEX` is rejected and the participant falls through to second-pass assignment at `>= 1`.
- **Palette constants (2 cases):** `MODERATOR_COLOR_INDEX === 0`, `COLOR_PALETTE_SIZE === 10`.
- **Re-exports from shared (2 cases):** `normalizeMentionName` and `mentionMatches` are both functions (confirms the re-export shape, not the function semantics — those are covered by the shared module's own tests).

Total: 21/21 pass.

#### GroupChatMessages retarget (cross-fork neutralization payoff)

`src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` lines 70-73 flip the import:

```
- } from '../../renderer/utils/participantColors';
+ } from '../utils/participantColors';
```

Surgical 2-byte edit (one path string). The retarget eliminates the cross-fork edge that the original `leaf-groupchat-messages` lift accepted as transitive surface. `npx vitest run src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.parity.test.ts` → 6/6 still pass (no behavioral regression). `grep 'renderer/utils/participantColors' src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` → empty (cross-fork edge gone).

The other five cross-fork imports inside `GroupChatMessages` (`textProcessing`, `markdownConfig`, `clipboard`, and the by-now-already-flipped `MarkdownRenderer`) stay deferred to later parade entries. This lift neutralizes specifically the `participantColors` edge.

#### Files added (NEW, additive only)

- `src/webFull/utils/participantColors.ts` — pure surface only (group 1 + group 2 + re-exports). 160 LOC including the header comment documenting the impure-functions omission.
- `src/webFull/utils/participantColors.test.ts` — 21 vitest cases across 5 describe-blocks.

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/utils/index.ts` — added a "Layer 2.5 leaf-parade primitives" section with the seven function exports + `ParticipantColorInfo` type-only export. No prior exports changed.
- `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` — 1 line changed (`'../../renderer/utils/participantColors'` → `'../utils/participantColors'`). The retarget that neutralizes the cross-fork edge.
- `ISA.md` — this Decision entry + the new `ISC-44.layer-2.5.participant_colors_util` line under the per-feature parity-catalog section directly as `[x]` CLOSED, placed before `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_messages` so the lift dependency reads top-down (the util is now an upstream of the messages view).

#### Files NOT touched

- `src/web/` — read-only oracle per fork hygiene.
- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle per fork hygiene.
- `src/main/` — no new server routes; the boundary surface is purely a renderer-side React lifecycle hook.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — `GitStatusWidget` lift)

Branch `leaf-git-status-widget` cut off `main @ 714337edf`. This lift ports the renderer's header git-status widget (244 LOC) into webFull. The widget is a header pill that displays git file changes with a GitHub-style hover tooltip — compact mode shows file count, full mode shows additions / deletions / modified breakdown, hover reveals per-file diff bars + "View Full Diff" / optional "View Git Log" actions.

#### Decisions

1. **`GitStatusWidget.tsx` — body-verbatim lift, hook self-source stripped → promoted to props.** Source (`src/renderer/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx`, 244 LOC) is a memoized presentational widget that self-sources from two focused contexts:

   ```ts
   const { getFileCount } = useGitFileStatus();
   const { getFileDetails } = useGitDetail();
   const fileCount = getFileCount(sessionId);
   const fileDetails = getFileDetails(sessionId);
   ```

   The provider behind those contexts (`GitStatusProvider` at `src/renderer/contexts/GitStatusContext.tsx`) is built on `useGitStatusPolling` (`src/renderer/hooks/git/useGitStatusPolling.ts`), which calls `window.maestro.git.getStatus(...)` at module-instantiation. Lifting the context as-is would drag the entire git-status polling hook + the IPC site through the webFull bundle entry point — out of scope per the brief's explicit guard: "If git status reads via IPC at module-load, STOP + report — needs a server-side route which is out of scope."

   The widget body itself, however, is IPC-clean: pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx` → empty (exit 1). The IPC site is one transitive hop away (in the context provider, not in the widget). So the lift is feasible if the hook self-source is severed at the lift boundary.

   Matching webFull pattern (per `AppOverlays` and `SessionList` L4.1 precedents): **promote the self-sourced values to props.** Two new inputs replace the hook calls:

   - `fileCount: number` — replaces `getFileCount(sessionId)`
   - `fileDetails?: GitFileDetails` — replaces `getFileDetails(sessionId)`

   The host (a downstream layer-wiring pass that ports the git-status substrate as a REST + WS surface) decides where those values come from: a future webFull `useGitFileStatus()` hook reading `/api/git/status`, a global store, or prop-drilling from the App root. The widget stays a pure render of `(fileCount, fileDetails, theme, callbacks)` with no implicit data dependencies. All render logic inside the component body is verbatim from the renderer source.

2. **`sessionId` prop dropped from the lifted surface.** The renderer source uses `sessionId` only to key into the two stripped hooks (`getFileCount(sessionId)` / `getFileDetails(sessionId)`). With the hooks gone, the widget no longer needs to know which session it's representing — that key is the host's responsibility. A future host that wants to surface "this widget is for session X" for debugging or analytics can wrap with `<div data-session-id={id}>` at the call site. This is consistent with the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` precedent of accepting only the data shape the widget actually renders.

3. **Type-resolution adapts (matching the L2.5 precedent):**

   - `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap; renderer aggregator routes through `src/renderer/types/index.ts` which re-exports from `src/shared/theme-types`).
   - `GitFileChange` is NOT pulled from `'../contexts/GitStatusContext'` (which re-exports it from `useGitStatusPolling`). The renderer's `GitFileChange` interface is small and stable (5 primitive fields: `path`, `status`, `additions`, `deletions`, `modified`). Instead, the lifted module defines it locally. This matches the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` / `DeleteWorktreeModal` precedent of pulling only the specific data shape each lifted module consumes, rather than copying the entire renderer hook + context graph into the webFull tree (which would drag the IPC site through the bundle, defeating the whole purpose of the lift).
   - A new `GitFileDetails` aggregate type captures the shape the renderer hook's `getFileDetails(sessionId)` returns: `{ fileChanges?: GitFileChange[], totalAdditions: number, totalDeletions: number, modifiedCount: number }`. The renderer declares this shape inline inside `GitDetailContextValue`; lifting it to a named type here keeps the prop contract greppable.

4. **`lucide-react` icons (`GitBranch`, `Plus`, `Minus`, `FileEdit`, `FileDiff`, `History`) kept verbatim** — already a webFull-tree dep used by other L2.5 lifts.

5. **Theme access pattern.** Kept the renderer's `theme: Theme` prop convention per the L2.1 / L2.3 / L2.4 / L2.5 precedent. Host calls `const { theme } = useTheme()` at the feature-component level and threads it down.

6. **Parity catalog scope.** Nine stories total (5 happy + 4 negative — meets the brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative" floor) covering:

   - Happy: compact-pill rendering with file count text + `title="+0 −0 ~0"` summary; full-breakdown rendering with additions / deletions / modified counts + summary title; tooltip listing changed files with per-file `+N` / `−N` counts on hover; "View Full Diff" affordance presence; "View Git Log" affordance presence when `onViewLog` is supplied.
   - Negative: suppression when `!isGitRepo` (no compact or full pill in DOM); suppression when `fileCount === 0` (even though `isGitRepo === true`); "View Git Log" hidden when `onViewLog` callback absent; lifecycle no-IPC / no-WS pin (the component does not reach into `window.maestro` or any transport — action callbacks are the caller's contract).

   Six catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3 happy stories, ≥1 negative-per-happy, allowed-verb-only, non-empty given/when/then, IPC-leak guard, and a presentational-contract pin that asserts the catalog never drifts toward `role="dialog"` assertions (the widget is a header pill + hover tooltip, not a modal — a future refactor wrapping in a modal is a behavior change and should fail the catalog rather than silently track it).

#### Files added (NEW, additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx` (body lifted verbatim from the 244-LOC renderer source; extended header documents the prop-promotion decision + the type-resolution adapts).
- `src/webFull/components/GitStatusWidget.parity.test.ts` (9 stories: 5 happy + 4 negative; 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended a `GitStatusWidget` block (component + `GitStatusWidgetProps` + `GitFileChange` + `GitFileDetails` type re-exports) under the existing Layer 2.5 leaf-parade section, after the `GroupChatPanel` line.
- `ISA.md` — appended this evidence block; added `ISC-44.layer-2.5.git_status_widget` directly as `[x]` CLOSED at the per-feature ISC list (line follows `ISC-44.layer-2.5.groupchat_panel` placement, ordered by lift sequence).

#### Files NOT touched

- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle. The renderer continues to render the renderer `GitStatusWidget` as part of the Electron entrypoint via its `useGitFileStatus()` / `useGitDetail()` hooks.
- `src/web/` — fork-hygiene read-only.
- `src/main/` — no new server routes; the widget surface is purely visual and prop-callback-driven. A future `/api/git/status` route is the prerequisite for actually wiring this widget into a webFull host, but that route is its own brief.
- `src/main/` — no new server routes; both lifted surfaces are purely visual and prop-callback-driven.
- `src/renderer/` — read-only oracle per fork hygiene. The renderer-side `participantColors.ts` remains the canonical home for `loadColorPreferences` / `saveColorPreferences`.
- `src/main/` — no new IPC handlers; this is a pure-util lift.
- `src/server/` — untouched.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- **Lifting `GitStatusContext` / `GitStatusProvider` / the `useGitStatusPolling` hook.** This is the IPC-bound substrate the widget self-sources from in the renderer; lifting it would require a server-side `/api/git/status` route (with polling cadence + per-session keying), a webFull-side hook to consume the route, and a WS frame to invalidate cached file details when files change. That is a multi-file architecture lift, explicitly out of scope per the brief's guard.
- **Wiring the lifted `GitStatusWidget` into a webFull header host.** The widget contract now reads `fileCount` and `fileDetails` from props; a future feature-wiring pass that mounts this widget in the webFull header will need the `/api/git/status` substrate above to source those props. Until then, the widget ships as a primitive available in the L2.5 export surface without a live consumer.
- **Lifting `GitFileChange` into a shared types module.** The interface is currently defined twice: once at `src/renderer/hooks/git/useGitStatusPolling.ts` line 36, and once at `src/webFull/components/GitStatusWidget.tsx` (the local mirror this lift adds). When the git-status substrate lifts, the canonical home for `GitFileChange` should be `src/shared/git-types.ts` (with both the renderer hook and the webFull widget importing from there). For now, the local mirror is the lowest-risk pattern and matches the `ExecutionQueueIndicator` precedent.
- Wiring the lifted `MaestroSilhouette` / `AnimatedMaestro` into a webFull Standing Ovation overlay or brand-header host — those consumers are downstream-layer scope and live in larger feature lifts (`AppOverlays` itself already landed at L2.5 and currently still resolves the renderer-source silhouette via cross-fork import; that import line will flip in a follow-up sweep after this lift lands).
- Wiring the lifted `TemplateAutocompleteDropdown` into a webFull `AgentPromptComposerModal` or the Auto Run document editor — both consumers need the template-autocomplete hook (`useTemplateAutocomplete`) wired through with browser-safe transitive deps (`useClickOutside`, `TEMPLATE_VARIABLES`), which is its own brief.
- Lifting `useTemplateAutocomplete` itself into `src/webFull/hooks/` — the hook is composable at module-load time but its full lift is a downstream-layer concern (it owns the autocomplete reducer and the click-outside wiring that this presentational dropdown delegates to).
- Wiring `loadColorPreferences` / `saveColorPreferences` into webFull — when a downstream consumer needs persisted color preferences, the right move is a webFull settings adapter (likely WS-backed against the server-side settings store) at that point in the port. Not part of this lift.
- Lifting the remaining cross-fork imports inside `GroupChatMessages` (`textProcessing`, `markdownConfig`, `clipboard`) — each is its own leaf-parade brief.
- Lifting `GroupChatInput` — the consumer this lift is precondition #2 for, per Architect audit #7. With this lift landed, the input lift's pre-flight on the messages-view dependency chain shrinks to the remaining four cross-fork imports.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 evidence (leaf-parade — three pure util lifts in one branch: `textProcessing` + `clipboard` + `terminalProseStyles`; drains the GCM cross-fork debt to zero)

**Closes:** ISC-44.layer-2.5.text_processing_util, ISC-44.layer-2.5.clipboard_util, ISC-44.layer-2.5.terminal_prose_styles_util.

**Branch:** `leaf-gcm-utils` (worktree at `../maestro-leaf-utils`).

#### Context

Three of the five remaining cross-fork `renderer/utils/` imports inside `src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` are pure leaves (or have a pure subset that can be cleanly extracted). The L2.5 parade has been chipping at them one at a time; this branch bundles the three pure-util lifts into a single landing because the lifts are independent and the test surfaces don't interact.

The post-lift state — and the headline outcome of this branch — is that `GroupChatMessages.tsx` now has ZERO cross-fork `renderer/` imports remaining. `grep -E "^import.*renderer/|from ['\"].*renderer/" src/webFull/components/GroupChatMessages.tsx` returns empty. The 5 occurrences of `renderer/` still in the file are all inside the header comment block documenting the original lift's context — the import surface is fully drained.

#### Lift 1 — `textProcessing` util (verbatim full lift)

**Pre-flight grep on `src/renderer/utils/textProcessing.ts`** for `window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]|ipcRenderer` → empty (exit 1). The renderer file is a fully pure module — no IPC, no Electron deps, no `window.maestro` references at any depth. Verbatim full lift, no signature changes.

**Lifted surface:** `processCarriageReturns`, `processLogTextHelper`, `filterTextByLinesHelper`, `getCachedAnsiHtml`, `clearAnsiCache`, `stripMarkdown`, and the `ANSI_CACHE_MAX_SIZE` constant. Only `stripMarkdown` is consumed by GroupChatMessages today; the rest port cleanly so they're pre-positioned for future webFull-side consumers (e.g. terminal-output rendering).

**Utility test** (`src/webFull/utils/textProcessing.test.ts`, 15 vitest cases):

- `stripMarkdown` (7 cases — exceeds the brief's ≥5 floor): bold/italic/strikethrough removal, inline-code backtick stripping, fenced code-block content extraction without fences, ATX-header + blockquote stripping, link + image markdown to visible text (documents the quirk that link regex runs before image regex, so `![alt](url)` collapses to `!alt` — verbatim renderer behavior preserved with an inline comment in the test), mixed-bullet normalization to leading dashes, numbered-list ordering preservation after normalization.
- `processCarriageReturns` (2 cases): last-non-empty-segment-after-\r semantics; lines without \r left untouched.
- `processLogTextHelper` (2 cases): bare bash/zsh prompt + empty-line filtering in terminal mode; pass-through in AI mode.
- `filterTextByLinesHelper` (4 cases): empty-query passthrough, plain-text include, regex exclude, invalid-regex fallback to plain text.

All 15 pass. One test was initially asserting the "wrong" stripMarkdown behavior on image markdown; the test runner caught it and the test was updated to match the renderer-verbatim behavior with an explanatory comment. That's a feature of the parity-via-tests approach — the test catches drift even on the first write.

#### Lift 2 — `clipboard` util (pure surface only; `safeClipboardWriteImage` deliberately NOT lifted)

**Pre-flight grep on `src/renderer/utils/clipboard.ts`** returned 1 hit: `await window.maestro.shell.copyImageToClipboard(dataUrl)` at line 48, inside the `safeClipboardWriteImage` function body, lambda-deferred via optional chaining (`if (window.maestro?.shell?.copyImageToClipboard)`).

The hit is at runtime inside a function body, NOT at module-load time. Per the same precedent that `leaf-groupchat-messages` used to accept `markdownConfig.ts`'s lambda-deferred `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` calls, this lift COULD have shipped the whole module — but the right move here is different: GroupChatMessages only uses `safeClipboardWrite` (text path). The image variant has no current webFull consumer, and the renderer's image-path implementation reaches for an Electron-only IPC bridge that webFull genuinely cannot fulfill. So the lift carries only the pure subset.

**Lifted surface:** `safeClipboardWrite` (pure `navigator.clipboard.writeText` wrapper that swallows `NotAllowedError`), `safeClipboardWriteBlob` (pure `navigator.clipboard.write` wrapper for binary clipboard items).

**NOT lifted:** `safeClipboardWriteImage`. The header comment-block documents the omission and notes the right moves when a webFull consumer needs image-to-clipboard support: (1) an explicit webFull adapter that calls the browser Clipboard API directly (the renderer's fallback path is already pure), or (2) a host-aware capability injection from the webFull entrypoint. Neither smuggles `window.maestro` into webFull.

**Utility test** (`src/webFull/utils/clipboard.test.ts`, 5 vitest cases — exceeds the brief's ≥3 floor):

- `safeClipboardWrite` (3 cases): success returns true and forwards text; `NotAllowedError` from `navigator.clipboard.writeText` returns false; `navigator.clipboard === undefined` returns false (vitest's jsdom env doesn't provide a writable clipboard, so the suite installs a mock via `Object.defineProperty` with `configurable: true` and restores via `afterEach`).
- `safeClipboardWriteBlob` (2 cases): success returns true and forwards `ClipboardItem[]`; rejection returns false.

All 5 pass.

#### Lift 3 — `terminalProseStyles` (surgical extract from `markdownConfig.ts`, NOT a full lift)

**Why surgical, not full.** `src/renderer/utils/markdownConfig.ts` is 925 LOC. It exports `generateProseStyles`, the `createMarkdownComponents` family (wizard bubble + release notes flavors), `generateAutoRunProseStyles`, `generateDiffViewStyles`, and the symbol we need — `generateTerminalProseStyles`. The file pulls in `react-markdown` `Components`, `react-syntax-highlighter`, the renderer-side `BionifyText` React component, and `getSyntaxStyle` from the theme registry. The wizard-bubble and release-notes factories contain `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` callsites inside their anchor `onClick` lambda bodies — lambda-deferred, but still a surface webFull would have to either tolerate or strip.

GroupChatMessages only consumes ONE symbol: `generateTerminalProseStyles(theme, scopeSelector) -> string`. That function is a pure CSS-string generator that reads `theme.colors` and concatenates a template literal. Its only external collaborator is `getBionifyReadingModeStyles` from `bionifyReadingMode.tsx`, which is ALSO a pure CSS-string generator (the rest of `bionifyReadingMode.tsx` is React components that this CSS function doesn't touch).

**Extract carries** (into the new `src/webFull/utils/terminalProseStyles.ts`):

- Constants matching the renderer defaults: `DEFAULT_BIONIFY_REST_OPACITY = 0.65`, `DEFAULT_BIONIFY_INTENSITY = 1`.
- `clamp` helper (3-line pure function, no need to import from anywhere).
- `resolveBionifyRestOpacity(intensity, theme?)` — pure helper, identical signature and body to the renderer source.
- `getBionifyReadingModeStylesCss(scopeSelector, theme?)` — pure CSS-string generator, byte-equivalent to the renderer's `getBionifyReadingModeStyles` for the `(scopeSelector, theme)` call shape used by `generateTerminalProseStyles`. Named with `Css` suffix locally to avoid shadowing the renderer-side React-component-injecting variant for readers comparing the two side-by-side.
- `generateTerminalProseStyles(theme, scopeSelector)` — verbatim CSS template from the renderer source line 833+.

**Extract OMITS:** the React-side `BionifyText` / `BionifyTextBlock` components, `transformBionifyNode` and friends, the style-injection side-effect (`hasInjectedBionifyStyles`), algorithm-parsing for runtime config, all other `generate*ProseStyles` functions, the `createMarkdownComponents` family, `generateDiffViewStyles`.

**Parity guarantee documented in the file header:** the CSS string the extract emits MUST match the renderer's output byte-for-byte for the same `(theme, scopeSelector)` inputs. If a future webFull port needs more of the markdown-config surface, the right move is a SECOND surgical extract — NOT a full module lift — so the Electron-only deps don't leak.

**Utility test** (`src/webFull/utils/terminalProseStyles.test.ts`, 5 vitest cases — exceeds the brief's ≥3 floor):

- Returns a non-empty CSS string scoped to the given selector + `.prose`.
- Emits theme colors for headings (h1=accent, h2=success, h3=warning), code backgrounds (`bgSidebar`), and accent-with-underline links.
- Includes the inlined Bionify reading-mode rules (`.bionify-word`, `.bionify-word-emphasis`, `.bionify-word-rest`) with the dark-theme default `--bionify-rest-opacity` of 0.65.
- Shifts the Bionify rest-opacity fallback for light-mode themes — `mode: 'light'` produces `var(--bionify-rest-opacity, 0.73)` (verifies the `resolveBionifyRestOpacity` branch on `theme?.mode === 'light'`).
- Scoping pin: every emitted rule selector begins with the provided scope prefix.

All 5 pass.

### 2026-06-08 — Layer 2.5 leaf-parade — `KeyboardMasteryCelebration` lift

#### Why this lift exists

Per the leaf-parade audit, `src/renderer/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.tsx` (350 LOC) is a leaf component — 0 IPC namespaces and 0 Electron-only API at module load (pre-flight `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]"` → empty, exit 1). It is the second of the three overlays referenced in `src/webFull/components/AppOverlays.tsx`'s file header to land in webFull, after `FirstRunCelebration` (`leaf-first-run-celebration` @ `fd9bc3cf9`). The L2.5 `AppOverlays` dispatcher accepts `keyboardMasterySlot: ReactNode | null` and gates rendering on `pendingKeyboardMasteryLevel !== null`; the slot was a deferral because the underlying component was renderer-only at the time. With this lift landed, the host wiring layer can pass `<KeyboardMasteryCelebration ... />` directly into `AppOverlays`'s `keyboardMasterySlot`, or keep the render-prop indirection (host's call — either choice is host-local; the dispatcher contract is stable).

`StandingOvationOverlay` remains the only deferred overlay of the three, because it carries a `window.maestro.shell.openExternal` callsite that would drag an IPC site through the webFull bundle entry point even lambda-deferred. That lift will need a webFull-side external-link surface (likely a `window.open(url, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer')` adapter under a feature flag) before it can land.

#### Import-path adapts (seven, all matching L2.5 precedent)

- `Theme` from `'../types'` → `'../../shared/theme-types'` (standard L2.5 swap — webFull has no `types/` aggregator that re-exports `Theme`; the renderer barrel itself routes through `src/renderer/types/index.ts` which re-exports from `src/shared/theme-types`).
- `Shortcut` from `'../types'` → `'../../renderer/types'` directly (the interface lives in the renderer types barrel only — `src/renderer/types/index.ts` — and is not yet replicated to `src/shared/`. Matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` / `GroupChatHeader` precedent of pulling specific types from the canonical renderer aggregator rather than copying into `src/shared/`. `Shortcut` is a pure data shape with no transitive `window.maestro` references).
- `useLayerStack` from `'../contexts/LayerStackContext'` resolves to the webFull-side context at `src/webFull/contexts/LayerStackContext.tsx` (lifted in L2.1).
- `MODAL_PRIORITIES` from `'../constants/modalPriorities'` resolves via the webFull re-export at `src/webFull/constants/modalPriorities.ts` (per Architect 2026-06-08 audit risk A — non-divergent constants stay re-exported from renderer to prevent silent drift). Uses `MODAL_PRIORITIES.KEYBOARD_MASTERY` (1095, just below `STANDING_OVATION` at 1100).
- `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS` from `'../constants/keyboardMastery'` → `'../../renderer/constants/keyboardMastery'`. The constants module is pure data (level definitions `{ id, name, threshold, description }`, zero IPC at module load — matches the L2.5 `ShortcutsHelpModal` precedent of pulling non-divergent renderer constants directly by relative path rather than duplicating into `src/shared/`).
- `DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS` from `'../constants/shortcuts'` → `'../../renderer/constants/shortcuts'`. Same rationale — pure data module (shortcut key arrays + metadata), zero IPC at module load. Used as the fallback when the optional `shortcuts` prop is not supplied.
- `isMacOSPlatform` from `'../utils/platformUtils'` resolves to the webFull-side shim at `src/webFull/utils/platformUtils.ts` which uses `navigator.userAgent` instead of the renderer's `window.maestro.platform` preload bridge. This is the same platform-detection divergence the L2.5 `shortcutFormatter` shim handles for other lifts.

The component's local `formatShortcutKeys(keys: string[], isMac: boolean)` helper is preserved verbatim from the renderer source — it takes a `(keys, isMac)` signature and joins without a separator (e.g. `['Meta', '/']` → `'⌘/'`), which is a different signature from the webFull `shortcutFormatter` shim's `formatShortcutKeys(keys, separator?)`. Keeping the helper local preserves source fidelity — the renderer uses this no-separator form intentionally for the shortcut hint copy ("Press ⌘/ to see all shortcuts").

#### Composition shape

Large celebration modal — does NOT compose the L2.1 `Modal` primitive directly because the renderer source builds bespoke DOM chrome (dark backdrop at z-index 99997, gradient header glow, animated bouncing icon, level-progress dot row, music-themed confetti palette with per-level intensity scaling, gradient dismiss button, level-specific message swap between `Keyboard` + "Level Up!" for levels 0-3 and `Trophy` + "Keyboard Maestro!" for level 4).

Confetti behavior preserved verbatim: per-level intensity table (50/100/200/300/500 particles for levels 0-4); `zIndex` stays at 99998 (between backdrop and modal). Maestro variant (`level === 4`) fires an extra delayed 100-particle gold-star burst at 300ms after mount. All confetti calls honour `prefers-reduced-motion` AND the `disableConfetti` prop. All timeouts are tracked in `timeoutsRef` and cleared on unmount to avoid leaking timers.

Layer-stack registration uses `MODAL_PRIORITIES.KEYBOARD_MASTERY` (1095) with `focusTrap: 'strict'`, `blocksLowerLayers: true`, `capturesFocus: true`, `ariaLabel: 'Keyboard Mastery Level Up Celebration'`, and routes Escape to `handleClose()`. Celebration-on-close pattern: clicking the dismiss button (or pressing Enter/Escape) sets `isClosing`, fires a second confetti burst, then calls `onClose()` after an 800ms animation delay. The Continue button label flips to "Onwards!" during the `isClosing` window — preserved verbatim from the renderer source.

#### Files added (all under `src/webFull/`)

- `src/webFull/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.tsx` (~470 LOC including extended file-header documenting the seven import-path adapts and the composition-shape rationale; ~350 LOC of source code verbatim from the renderer).
- `src/webFull/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.parity.test.ts` (~290 LOC, 10 stories + 6 catalog-shape vitest guards).

#### Files modified (additive only)

- `src/webFull/components/index.ts` — appended `export { KeyboardMasteryCelebration } from './KeyboardMasteryCelebration';` immediately after the `FirstRunCelebration` export to keep the L2.5 leaf exports grouped by lift wave.

#### Files NOT touched

- `src/web/` — zero bytes diff vs main.
- `src/renderer/` — zero bytes diff vs main (read-only oracle).
- `src/main/` — zero bytes diff vs main.
- `src/server/` — zero bytes diff vs main.

#### Parity catalog

`src/webFull/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.parity.test.ts` declares 10 stories (5 happy + 5 negative — meets brief's "≥3 happy + ≥1 negative-per-happy" floor). Happy-path stories cover:

1. The standard "Level Up!" variation chrome (dialog with the canonical `aria-label="Keyboard Mastery Level Up"`, level name + description from `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS`, Continue button).
2. The next-level encouragement copy ("Keep using shortcuts to reach <next>") with dismiss hint.
3. The level-progression dot row rendering.
4. The Maestro variation at `level === 4` swapping title to "Keyboard Maestro!" + "the highest level" subhead + "You've mastered all keyboard shortcuts!" encouragement copy.
5. The level=0 boundary case (Beginner tier — pin against future refactors that use `if (level)` instead of explicit `level === 4`).

Negative-path stories cover:

1. Continue button → unmounts the dialog after the 800ms close-animation.
2. Escape key → same close path via layer-stack `onEscape`.
3. Backdrop click → close (with the card's `onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}` preserved so card-clicks DO NOT close).
4. No "Keep using shortcuts to reach the next level" copy at Maestro (the next-level branch must NOT render at level 4).
5. No "Level Up!" title at Maestro (the standard branch must NOT render at level 4).

Uses only the allowed assertion vocabulary (`hasElement`, `hasText`, `wsFrameMatches`, `dbHasRow`, `fsHas`, `processHas`, `notificationFired`, `broadcast`). Catalog-shape vitest guards: ≥3-story floor, ≥3-happy-path floor, ≥1-negative-per-happy floor, allowed-verbs guard, non-empty given/when/then, no-IPC-leakage guard. 6/6 in-suite vitest guards green.

#### Verification

- **Pre-flight on the renderer source:** `grep -E "window\.maestro\.|from ['\"]electron['\"]" src/renderer/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.tsx` → empty (exit 1).
- **Lint:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run lint` → clean (after `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npm run build:prompts` to materialize the pre-existing `src/generated/prompts.ts`).
- **Parity test:** `MAESTRO_HEADLESS=1 npx vitest run src/webFull/components/KeyboardMasteryCelebration.parity.test.ts` → PASS, 6/6 in-suite vitest guards green.
- **Scope-guard `git diff`s:** `git diff main..HEAD -- src/web/ src/renderer/ src/main/ src/server/ | wc -c` → 0 (read-only oracles + main + server untouched).
- **Symlink hygiene:** `node_modules` symlinked to `/Users/trilliumsmith/code/maestro/node_modules` for the lint/test run; removed before commit so the worktree stays clean.
- **Push status:** NOT pushed per brief instruction. Branch sits locally at `leaf-keyboard-mastery`, awaiting Trillium's merge.

#### Deferred / out-of-scope for this brief

- Wiring the lifted `KeyboardMasteryCelebration` into `src/webFull/App.tsx` (directly or through `AppOverlays`'s `keyboardMasterySlot`). That host-wiring pass needs the level-transition source wired (either a webFull-side modal-data store with a `pendingKeyboardMasteryLevel: number | null` field, or REST-backed `useSettings()` for the mastery-percentage threshold-crossing detector, plus the `useSettingsStore` `shortcuts` + `disableConfetti` reads — all renderer-only architecture today). Each of those is its own downstream-layer brief.
- Lifting `StandingOvationOverlay` — the third and final overlay referenced in `AppOverlays.tsx`'s file header. Pre-flight grep returns 1 hit (`window.maestro.shell.openExternal` inside the badge external-link affordance). Its lift will need a webFull-side external-link surface before it can land verbatim.
- Lifting `useModalStore` / `useSettingsStore` into webFull — needed for the host-wiring pass to source `keyboardMasteryData` and `shortcuts` / `disableConfetti` without prop-drilling from the App root. Multi-file architectural lift, explicitly out of scope per the brief's guard.
- Lifting `KEYBOARD_MASTERY_LEVELS` and `DEFAULT_SHORTCUTS` into `src/shared/` — both are non-divergent pure-data modules and could move to `src/shared/` as a future hygiene pass, but doing so would touch the renderer's import paths (the renderer-side files would need to be retargeted) which violates the "read-only renderer" rule. The cross-fork relative-path import is the lowest-risk pattern and matches the L2.5 precedent (`ShortcutsHelpModal`, `MarkdownRenderer`, etc.).
